Dinghai Pomfret Boats Robbed Again 159

Water Police Second Division Ordered to Patrol

Dinghai Li Port is surrounded by the sea, and most residents rely on fishing for a living. From Qingming Festival to the end of Great Heat, it is called the "Ocean Life Season," and fishermen are divided into two groups: one group catches yellow croaker, and the other catches pomfret. This year's fishing season is very prosperous. Fishermen Bei Xiyuan and Sun Aji, who belonged to the pomfret group, caught thousands of catties of pomfret and planned to transport it to Ningbo for sale. However, when they reached the waters of Dinghai, they were robbed. The people and the boat were taken to Taizhou, and they were only released after a huge ransom was paid. The remaining pomfret had already been auctioned off by the bandits. There are 130 yellow croaker boats and 53 pomfret boats in the port. Upon hearing this news, everyone felt insecure. The fishermen sent Wang Asheng to the Second Marine Police Brigade to petition. After receiving the report, the brigade dispatched the Second Division to patrol the area, ordering the arrest of the escaped bandits within a limited time.

Rioters Shoot Two Police Officers 162

Yesterday morning at 4:20 AM, Hu Yuzhen, patrol officer No. 2528 of the Central Police Station, and Shen Chaojia, patrol officer No. 3314 from Zhenjiang, were patrolling on Jiujiang Road when they saw two men hurrying past the public warehouse. Suspecting their behavior, they quickly pursued them. One officer grabbed one of the men from behind and began a search. Unexpectedly, the other man seized the opportunity, while the officers were unprepared, and pulled out a pistol, firing a shot at officer No. 2528, hitting him in the left wrist. The officer fell to the ground. Officer No. 3314, seeing this, bravely stepped forward to arrest the man, but the gunman fired twice at officer No. 3314, hitting him in the left wrist, causing him to fall to the ground as well. The two rioters then calmly escaped. Nearby officers, hearing the alarm, rushed to the scene to give chase, but to no avail. The injured officers were taken to Huade Road Hospital for treatment. Due to the suddenness of the event, the description of the two male rioters was not clear. It was only remembered that the gunman was about thirty years old and wearing a black cloth short shirt and trousers. The police station has launched a thorough search.

Demanding Gambling Debts Leads to Murder 164

Mao Jichang, a 27-year-old from Ningbo, worked at the duck slaughterhouse operated by Weng Qiyin at No. 88 Huiguan Street, Dongjiadu, Nanshi. A few days ago, he and his fellow villagers, nicknamed Da Lai and Hemp Skin, gathered to play mahjong. At that time, Mao owed Da Lai Hemp Skin three yuan in gambling debts. Mao had already paid back five jiao, still owing two yuan and five jiao. Da Lai Hemp Skin repeatedly demanded payment without success. Yesterday afternoon around 4:00 PM, Da Lai went to the duck slaughterhouse again to demand the outstanding debt, but still received no payment. Da Lai became increasingly angry and argued with Mao, which soon escalated into a conflict. In a fit of rage, Da Lai punched Mao hard in the waist. Unexpectedly, the blow hit a vital spot, and Mao fell to the ground, unmoving. Realizing he had caused a major disaster, Da Lai immediately fled. Mao's colleagues, Ye Aliang and others, heard the noise and rushed out, only to find Mao lying in the courtyard, pale-faced, breathing rapidly, and bleeding from all seven orifices. Knowing he was seriously injured, they quickly took him to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. However, due to the severity of the injury, he died before receiving treatment. They reported the situation to Yi, the chief of the first precinct's first station. Upon receiving the report, Yi, recognizing that this was a matter of life and death, ordered his subordinates to pursue the murderer and instructed Qin Defang, the local chief of the 23rd police division, to report the incident to the local court for an autopsy.

Police Strictly Crack Down on Lotteries 165

Wen Hong'en, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, previously discovered that lotteries were rampant in Nanshi and Zhabei, and their popularity was due to the strict prohibition by the French Concession authorities, leading them to secretly operate in the Chinese area under the guise of literary societies and poetry riddles. In reality, they were disguised lotteries, and these hooligans even brazenly claimed that certain government agencies had provided financial support. This bold and reckless behavior was intolerable. He issued a sincere proclamation, strictly prohibiting them, and ordered all district stations and teams to arrest them, with the goal of eradicating them completely. As a result, the number of cases cracked by various district stations has been increasing daily. However, to avoid arrest, the lottery organizers have devised various ingenious methods, such as collecting lottery gambling funds in latrines or urinals, or using newspaper vendors' bags to collect them in alleys. The methods are ever-changing, making arrests difficult. Yesterday, Shen Zhenhua, chief of the Second District's First Sub-Station, learned that the rascal Feng Bojin and Wang Weigen had established a large lottery operation at No. 9, Shi Cheng Lane. He dispatched Inspector Luo to lead police officers to make the arrest, capturing Feng and Wang and seizing gambling funds of seven yuan, 70 cents in corner tickets, fifteen double-corner coins, ninety lottery books, three small stamps, and eight hundred copper coins. They were all taken to the station. Additionally, Inspector Zhang Zeqian of Shipin Lane led police officers to investigate and arrest Zhao Asi, a lottery operator, in Daoxing Lane, seizing a bundle of lottery paper. Furthermore, Officer Qi led police officers to investigate and discover a lottery operation on the upper floor of the Tiger Stove in Monk Hong's residence, seizing thirty-one sheets of lottery paper. After interrogation, they were all sent to the General Bureau for legal action.

Song Chunfang's "Monte Carlo" 166

The writer Song Chunfang resigned from his position as a counselor at the Qingdao Municipal Government last autumn and joined the Shanghai Bank in this city. In his spare time, he wrote travelogues, which soon accumulated into a large volume. Recently, at the urging of his literary friends, he compiled and published them into a book. It is divided into six parts: France, Italy, Austria, Hungary, Switzerland, and China, with twelve travelogues in total. Those belonging to France include "Monte Carlo," "Paris (1)," and "Paris (2)." The Italian section has "Venice," the Austrian section has "Innsbruck" and "Schloss Itter," the Hungarian section has "Budapest," the Swiss section has "Geneva (1)" and "Geneva (2)," and the Chinese section has "Beijing," "Hangzhou (1)," and "Hangzhou (2)." The book is named after the first travelogue, "Monte Carlo." Monte Carlo is the world's premier gambling destination, renowned throughout the world. If you want to know its contents, you must read Mr. Song's book. The copyright of this book has been purchased by the China Travel Service at a high price, and it has been beautifully printed and published. The cover was designed by Mr. Ye Gongchao, which adds to the book's charm. Each copy sells for eight jiao. It is available at the China Travel Service in this and other cities, as well as at major bookstores on the Fourth Road.

Newly Published Chahar Map 167

Despite the Tanggu Truce, the Japanese army is still moving troops into Chahar. The area is located on the automobile road from Zhangjiakou north to Outer Mongolia's Kulun, a vital trade route between China and Russia. Furthermore, the three provinces of Rehe, Chahar, and Suiyuan are all located outside the Great Wall, in what was formerly Inner Mongolia. The Japanese covet Manchuria and Mongolia. Although they have temporarily acquired our four northeastern provinces, their ambition to gain an inch and then a foot is still focused on Chahar and Suiyuan. Each copy only costs three jiao for paper materials, and stamps are accepted. Send a letter and it will be sent immediately.

Reader's Advisory

How to Return to the "Motherland"? 184

丨Letter from Ban Yu from Nanyang Sand and Sarawak丨

Advisor,

Most of the overseas Chinese here were forced to come because of extortion by local bullies and gentry in the motherland, accounting for about 40-50%. Among those who earned money and returned home, 20-30% still suffered exploitation. Because of this, I am in a dilemma. I was born in a village often bullied by local tyrants. In the winter of the eighteenth year of the Republic of China, I was kidnapped by a local gentry in the city, in collusion with the army! I had to give him 10,000 yuan to escape! As a result, my family business went bankrupt, and I was heavily in debt! I had no choice but to leave my parents, who were over half a century old, and my young wife and children, and come to Nanyang to make a living. Fortunately, heaven has not failed me. When I first arrived in Sand and Sarawak, I was introduced by a friend and obtained a decent job. The treatment is good, and the salary is considerable. But it has been more than four years now. The debts I owed before have been gradually paid off, and my current job is also coming to an end. At this time, I should go home to visit my relatives, but I am afraid that I will still suffer at the hands of local bullies! It is really worrying and hesitant. But there is no Chinese consulate here to issue a passport, and I am not an intellectual who can ask the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission for protection. So I dare not decide to go back. Please, sir, help me find a safe way.

Answer:

Your family property was taken away by domestic bullies and bandits, and you found a job in Nanyang. In the reporter's opinion, it is better to live there. What value does the so-called "motherland" have that makes you yearn for it? The four northeastern provinces are discarded like worn-out shoes (in reality, not just in words), so how can there be the mood to care about overseas Chinese who are adrift? And how can there be the mind to care about you, a lonely, insignificant, poor scholar? As for us, we are very ashamed, we can't help you either. We can only hope that you will work hard and fight for yourself.

Zhu Qiu, Zou, Zhang Zhongxiong: Please indicate your address and attach a stamp so that we can send the reply. In the future, readers who write to us must provide a clear and detailed address and attach sufficient return postage for a reply. Also, please do not send letters regarding medical inquiries.

Shen Bao Domestic Goods Weekly

Intangible Losses 185

— Yang An

Intangible losses are the great enemy of domestic goods year. Not only are they the great enemy of domestic goods year, but all domestic goods factories, domestic goods companies, and even those who engage in all domestic goods businesses, suffer great losses from intangible losses. If readers don't believe it, let me give a few examples.

㈠ A good factory, the manager does not study the personnel problem too much, and is not good at controlling the workers, so that the workers go from hope to complaint to resentment, so more coal is burned. Motors and gasoline are wasted, materials are wasted, and goods are secretly stolen. Obviously, the business is very prosperous and the interest is very high, but the result is a loss of money. What is the reason? It lies in this intangible loss.

㈡ A good domestic goods store, at first, all the clerks were full of energy and enthusiasm for business. The manager wore nearsighted glasses, only looking at the immediate and one-sided, and the treatment was a little harsh. The clerks put on "old master faces" and dealt with customers lazily. The customer asks a question, and he reluctantly answers it. The customer wants an item, and he reluctantly takes it out. Originally, dealing with customers was all-round, answering all questions, and asking about all items. At that time, the customer only wanted one item, but he was happy to be asked and bought three or four items. Now the clerks' mentality is that they only hope that customers ask less to avoid trouble and annoyance. The manager thinks that the disposal is appropriate, but why don't you go and see the faces of your subordinates? Hurry up and look further and expand your measure? This is also an intangible loss.

㈢ A factory, a store, an organization, all losses are often due to the lack of a plan, a budget. A printed item is printed a lot, and as a result, a large amount of printing costs are thrown into the wastepaper basket and sold as waste newspapers. There is also an organization that prints irrelevant things horizontally and vertically every day. Others throw it in the wastepaper basket, but it takes effort and wastes resources to do this unjust thing. What is the benefit? There is also tap water that is opened carelessly, and electric lights that are used indiscriminately. Partners and students think that this is public property, so they don't care. However, this intangible loss is countless.

㈣ To get rich, everything can be done. Why don't you do this and don't do that, but you have to sell Japanese goods? For one person to get rich, the result is to harm domestic goods manufacturers, harm social economy, and harm national strength. He thinks that he is doing it secretly, without anyone knowing, as long as he can deceive people and earn money, what else does he care about? It is a pity that Shanghai is doing unconscionable things all day long, all year round by these bastards. How can any mathematician calculate this intangible loss?

Domestic Goods Talk

Upholding the Implementation of the New Tariff 186

— Xuan Wan

A country's officially promulgated tariff rules are, by their very nature, already established, and there is no need to say anything like "upholding" to promote their implementation. However, in our weak country, under the initial promulgation of this new tariff, there have been attempts to obstruct it, which is unreasonable and painful. Originally, our country has been heavily bound by the lack of tariff autonomy for decades. Imperialists rely on all unequal treaties as a protective charm, pushing all surplus production to all parts of our country, seeking the highest profits with the lowest tax rates, and vigorously dumping and plundering. But on the other hand, they raise export taxes, causing our country's exports to suffer a heavy blow, and the decline in foreign trade is increasing, creating an unprecedented increase in the amount of trade deficit, destroying the development of the entire industrial and commercial future, and gradually forming a situation of the guest overwhelming the host. The current decline in our foreign markets and various financial and economic panics can all be attributed to the impact of tariffs over the years, and the astonishing loss of resources. Looking back on the past, we naturally cannot bear to look back. Now that the government has recovered autonomy for many years, May 6 of this year is also the day when the forced signing of the one-sided beneficial Sino-Japanese reciprocal tariff agreement expires. Looking at the world's countries building high tariff barriers to drive out foreign goods, so that imported goods have no foothold, then the implementation of our new tariff this time can at least hope to eliminate old obstacles and promote the sales of domestic goods (in fact, the regulations of this new tariff, although slightly increased, are still far from the world's countries). However, this cunning and insidious Japanese imperialism, disregarding public reason, still wants to coerce. Recently, it is widely rumored that the local Japanese Chamber of Commerce convened a general meeting, gathered to discuss, drafted a letter of request, handed it to the Japanese envoy Arima, and forwarded it to our country's authorities, making unreasonable demands. Their absurd actions and illegal acts have been openly exposed. Tariff autonomy is a common practice in all countries, and the promulgation of tariffs is a matter of internal affairs. Does Japan, which claims to be civilized (?), still not understand this international common sense? Disregarding national rights, what is their intention? If this can be tolerated, what cannot be tolerated? Although the National Goods Production and Sales Cooperation Association and various national goods organizations have repeatedly telegraphed the central government to support it, all citizens should unite and rise up to be the support. They deeply know that the increase or decrease of tax rates is the biggest key to promoting national goods and resisting enemy goods, and it is also the key to the rise and fall of industry. Life is related, how can we ignore it? For our own survival and for the sovereignty of the country, we hope that the government will refute according to reason, strictly refuse, and carry out its original intention without any concessions, in order to maintain sovereignty and cultivate the foundation of the country. Then, of course, not only will it be beneficial to the future of our national goods, but also the basis for the economic revival of the entire people's livelihood.

"Bargain," "Sacrifice," and Others 187

— Ke Ding'an

"Genuine goods at a fair price" is a saying that comes from old businessmen; but new businessmen of the times must also regard it as a standard. For example, a rice store, the price of the rice you sell is balanced, whether it is white glutinous rice or brown glutinous rice, as long as people buy it to cook rice, it has good swelling properties and few impurities, then people will always trust you, and in the future, they will not go to other stores to buy rice. Looking at the above example, these four words "genuine goods at a fair price" can show its effectiveness.

Shanghai is a prosperous city, with shops lined up and dense smoke. Compared with other famous cities, it is even more so. Therefore, those engaged in the national goods business are also setting up factories in Shanghai to produce and promote their sales. It can almost be said that "China's well-known factories are all gathered in Shanghai."

I don't know who was the first person to create it? 丨丨 Forgive me for not being able to find out its origin, 丨丨 is the one who created "big bargains." When he created it, I also knew that it was because the market was not good, and he used "big bargains" as a call. Sure enough, after the news of "big bargains" was revealed in the newspaper, their business was unexpected. Compared with ordinary days, the total number of businesses exceeded several times. This is certainly due to "big bargains."

"Making money" is the most common idea of a businessman. With such a good shortcut to make money, who would be willing to give up? 丨 So one person imitates it, and a hundred people follow it. At first, it was only limited to Shanghai, and slowly spread to towns and major cities. This shortcut to make money is known all over the country.

When the three words "big bargain" gradually lost their effectiveness, smart merchants used their brains to come up with what: "sacrifices," "cheap goods," and what else: "special sacrifices," "very cheap goods," etc. to call on general buyers. At first, it seemed like taking morphine, which was somewhat effective, but later it felt that there was no response. So they used the method of "wool comes from the sheep" to "big gifts," but it could not last forever and would always be eliminated.

Today, the national crisis is getting deeper and the foreign insults are getting more urgent. The great business community 丨丨 including all the ports in the country 丨 are holding × quarter big bargains, special big bargains, × week anniversary big bargains one after another because of the poor business. You are holding them like this, and they are also holding them like this. On one street, almost the eastern side is beating, and the western side is banging, making the ears of the walking people deafening. In principle, with such grand publicity, the business income

should exceed the usual: but after careful investigation, it will even drop below the usual total business volume. What is the reason for this? Half of it is of course that the market is not good, and the purchasing power of ordinary people is weakening accordingly: half of it is because most stores deceive themselves and cannot gain the trust of ordinary patrons, and even some stores with short-sighted eyes hire people to pull and pull at the door. This is even more losing the rules of the store. I think that those who have local responsibilities, if they don't add restrictions, I am afraid it will create an even worse situation, right? In the near future, you will blow your own horn, and I will ignore and not buy. What kind of panic will it become at that time? It's hard to describe.

I think that stores that specialize in selling domestic goods, or large department stores, should especially prohibit new and unique ideas, and should not follow the trend and imitate others. You must know that the sale of domestic goods depends entirely on uniform pricing, 丨丨 what I said

uniform, is based on the lowest standard price, 丨丨 to gain the trust of buyers. Not long ago, just talking about two-pound thermos bottles, some stores' lowest price was one yuan per bottle, then 95 cents, 85 cents, 80 cents, and some people followed the price drop. Now some people are selling them for 75 cents, 丨 these thermos bottles are all domestic goods, 丨 may I ask, is the cost of a two-pound thermos bottle for 75 cents enough? In this way, isn't it going to lose money? A friend said to me like this: "They lose this, earn that, and average it out to still make money." Business secrets, each has its own. There is nothing wrong with investigating. However, such a reduction in pricing and confusion in the market is really unjustified. Therefore, I think that to improve business and gain the trust of society, it is definitely not enough to rely solely on "big bargains" or "big sacrifices" "big gifts." The fundamental and proper method is still to think about "uniform pricing," "small profits," "superior goods," and "no crazy boasting." If you can do this, in the first one or two months, ordinary people will of course not all know it because they are used to buying cheap goods. I think that now ordinary people have a comparative concept when buying things. They see that the goods you sell are cheaper than the big bargains of others, and the goods are more beautiful; then by their oral propaganda, 丨丨 you must know that the effect of oral propaganda is the greatest! 丨丨 In less than half a year, your total monthly business volume will definitely be considerable. At the same time, the slogan "Practice using domestic goods" can be popularized throughout the country, and in the newspapers, you will not see the shocking news of "increased imports of foreign goods."

Domestic Goods Discussion

Regarding the Mobile Promotion of Domestic Goods 188

— Zhou Chengzhu

The call for a domestic goods exhibition is constantly shaking our eardrums. But after a careful examination, apart from the China National Goods Exhibition held a few years ago, and the Henan Mobile Exhibition that traveled thousands of miles and did some enthusiastic work, other exhibitions in the east and exhibitions in the west are either hastily held in a few thatched sheds, or completely occupied by vendors. Moreover, some manufacturers are holding the idea of profiteering, so the effect is really limited.

This kind of domestic goods exhibition that only promotes in the city and does not instill the concept of domestic goods to the upper-level people is really a superficial waving of flags and shouting. In the metropolis, everyone is shouting loudly, but the countryside is still indifferent. We try to see how many kinds of foreign medicines and cosmetics, they do not hesitate to paint large advertisements everywhere in the interior at cost, and even hire small steamships to drive directly to the countryside to half-sell and half-buy. This kind of selling method that has the heart of sacrifice and is different from others is indeed worthy of reference for those engaged in the domestic goods business.

Several domestic goods traveling groups once did some mobile promotion work for a while. They cooperated with local

Page 14

Administrative and educational institutions also used anti-Japanese films to help and strong publicity. We are very happy with the hard work they used, but lately it seems not as energetic as before. It is a pity that they lack sufficient economic resources and do not have a central meaning. The biggest reason is that the factories have become passive and do not have sufficient strength to help them, so that a few people shout themselves hoarse, eat and sleep in the open, and as a result, their spirits are scattered and their efforts are wasted.

Therefore, I believe that to measure the meat and land of the domestic goods mobile promotion countryside, and hope that the people can get a deep image, the only first move is to first actively gather from various famous domestic goods manufacturers, prepare sufficient economic strength, and sufficient talent ideas, and wash away the previous malpractices of the exhibition that were hastily perfunctory, and really work hard.

The level of knowledge and discrimination of the people is very shallow. They can hardly distinguish between domestic goods and non-domestic goods. Moreover, due to the recent collapse of the rural economy, it is easy to be fooled into buying enemy goods at low prices for use. In this year, the promotion and promotion of domestic goods to the interior countryside depends entirely on the use of simple signs and ordinary methods. Otherwise, using the sophisticated methods of the city to call on the public to use them will definitely fail.

Secondly, the mobile promotion of domestic goods is not just about running the wharf-style circling and boasting. It should bear the task of investigating the local market conditions, economic conditions, and the trend of domestic goods. It should not only work with local stores, but also provide detailed guidance to merchants on all good steps in operating and selling domestic goods, in order to achieve a close relationship between "production," "marketing," and "sales."

I would like to contribute the above paragraph to the gentlemen who are recently preparing for the mobile promotion of domestic goods.

Domestic Goods Investigation

The Realm of Domestic Goods 189

— Yu Chang

My country, with its vast land and abundant resources, has a very wide range of so-called domestic goods. But from the perspective of nature, it can be summarized as the following categories:

(1) Local products from all over the country.

(2) Industrial products manufactured with domestic raw materials, domestic capital, and manpower.

(3) Goods made with domestic capital and manpower, plus foreign raw materials.

(4) Goods manufactured by overseas Chinese.

The first two items are pure domestic goods, and there is no doubt about it. The last two items, if not explained, may cause suspicion. Among the relatives and friends of the reporter, there are those who have questioned this, so I will briefly describe my humble opinion below for the readers of this publication to discuss.

My country's industry has not yet developed, and many of the raw materials used by manufacturers are supplied by foreign merchants. Such as steel, such as aluminum, such as dyes, Taiwanese rayon, such as fragrances in cosmetics, such as the enamel color of enamelware, such as the hardening oil of soap, such as the paper pulp of papermaking, such as the carbolic acid of artificial ivory, my country cannot manufacture them ourselves. We hope that these raw materials can gradually be replaced by domestic products, so as to become complete domestic goods. However, before there are substitutes, being able to use foreign raw materials to process and manufacture, so as to resist the finished products of foreign merchants, its benefit to the national economy and people's livelihood is already not small. Can we say that those are not domestic goods?

Overseas Chinese, empty-handed, under the oppression of foreign governments, rely on their own blood and sweat to establish an economic foundation. Every year, they remit a part of their income back to the motherland, which invisibly makes up for a huge outflow of cash in my country's foreign trade. Moreover, their patriotism is far beyond what domestic compatriots can reach. Throughout history, for revolution, for domestic construction, and for the war of resistance against foreign aggression, the amount of money they have donated is in the tens of millions. The businesses they have created overseas, such as Chen Jiageng's rubber industry in Singapore, Yong An Tang's medicines in Yangon, and the swallow's nests of overseas Chinese merchants in Siam. The socks and shirts woven by overseas Chinese in Nanyang, the mats woven by overseas Chinese in Borneo, and the ginseng planted by overseas Chinese merchants in the Americas can all be transported to China and become powerful enemies of foreign goods. Therefore, the goods manufactured by overseas Chinese can be said to be genuine domestic goods, and domestic goods stores in various parts of the country should do their best to promote them, which should not be denied by anyone.

The Way of Women 190

— Quan

Men have the "way of husbands," so why don't women have the "way of women"?

The so-called women, as the name suggests, are of course the figures of the housewife class, not young girls.

The housewife is the "Minister of Internal Affairs" in the family, and at the same time she also serves as the "Minister of Finance." Her greatness and the importance of her responsibilities can be imagined.

One person concurrently holds two important positions, whether in theory or in fact, must be "of one heart and one mind" and "must be loyal"

to do it. What's more, in the current unprecedented environment of crisis!

The wheels of the times are moving forward relentlessly, and now we have reached the final critical period of the world. Famine, unemployment, and recession are spreading all over the world.

Steel-like facts have been presented to everyone. No one can deny it, and no one can ignore it

!

For this unprecedented personal prosperity and danger, the enlightened women of various countries are urgently implementing coping strategies.

For their own existence and the prosperity of the country and society, they work diligently and frugally, striving to increase income,

and striving for perfection in frugality, striving to reduce expenses. They do not buy a penny of foreign goods, and they advocate domestic goods.

Don't you believe it? Let me give you a few examples!

Have you ever seen Japanese or Russian women spend a penny to buy our valuable goods?

No, no, they would not do this even if they were burned to ashes.

Have you ever seen them indulging in pleasure and wandering all day long?

No, no, they only have work forever! Work! Work!

This is their "way of women."

At the same time, we certainly hope that it will also be the "way of Chinese women"!

Promoting Domestic Goods to the Interior 191

— Xu Nangong

The universalization of domestic goods in the interior is the urgent need of the moment, and it is also the common goal of the domestic goods industry. Although there are now many enthusiastic people who are actively organizing domestic goods mobile promotion groups, domestic goods traveling groups, domestic goods mobile propaganda groups, etc., they are tirelessly traveling to various parts of the interior to promote exhibitions. Their deep intentions and painstaking efforts, a spirit of fighting for domestic goods, really make us admire them very much.

Here I have a small opinion, which is also my ideal. I am afraid that the smart gentlemen have already seen it, but it may be useful for our mutual exploration. Of course, their current organization is very necessary, but I think that mobile propaganda can only attract the attention of the people in the interior and make them aware of it for a while. It cannot permanently make them understand and supply their needs. It is a passive promotion, not a thorough and fundamental promotion, because mobile work is only stationed in a city or town for a month or ten days to display and sell, and the goods needed by the people cannot be purchased as much as possible in this extremely short period of time, especially in this period of weak rural economy. How can they have the ability to pre-purchase and prepare goods that are not urgently needed for the time being?

Facts tell us that the material enjoyment of the people in the interior, in addition to a part of the self-reliant earth cloth vegetable rice they use, other daily necessities are purchased from nearby towns, and most of the general shops are for profit, and those with patriotic ideas are very rare. Therefore, the goods purchased by the shops from larger cities or metropolises, regardless of whether they are domestic goods, foreign goods, or even inferior goods, only take the low spring price for sale. Therefore, although the people in the interior have patriotic enthusiasm to use domestic goods, they have to purchase them nearby because there is nowhere to inquire. Therefore, the difficulty of domestic goods penetrating into the interior is mostly manipulated by general merchants, forming a separation between producers and consumers!

Now that we have seen the above malpractices, we must find ways to remedy them. The prudent and meticulous road to instill domestic goods into the interior will have many people's planning. Now I will write down the follies of my mind.

Gather funds to create domestic goods general stores or companies in important cities (such as Shanghai, Tianjin, etc.), and set up branch stores in various cities and towns, distributing them according to the size of the market and the convenience of transportation, so that the interior and the city are connected as one, and sign sales contracts with various domestic goods factories, purchasing in large quantities at the lowest price, distributing them to various branch stores, selling them at low prices to reduce the burden on the people, and using shipping vessels for the transportation of goods (such as shipping vessels in various places) to distribute them to branch stores. If so, there will be no shortage of goods needed in the interior, and there will be no worries about the sales of production factories, connecting the supply and demand of producers and consumers, removing the separation between the interior and the city, and further familiarizing themselves with local customs and habits and improving them, there will be great benefits for the future of domestic goods.

Although this organization is similar to a domestic goods introduction center, etc., one is aimed at the capitals of various provinces, and the other is focused on the rural areas of the interior. The methods are the same, but the intentions are different. It is called each doing their best and each showing their strengths.

Our Country's Mosquito Coil Industry (Part 1) 192

— Songlu

As the weather gradually gets warmer, those detestable mosquitoes will soon come in swarms to wreak havoc. Let us not neglect these small creatures, as they not only disturb our sweet dreams and suck our blood, but also spread malaria, creating a terrifying society! To maintain peaceful sleep and protect their physical safety, humans have had to devise ways to drive them away and exterminate them. Thus, the mosquito coil has become a necessity for summer.

Twenty years ago, our country did not have safe and effective mosquito coils. The ones sold in the market were nothing more than locally made mosquito coils rolled from wood shavings and sulfur. These mosquito coils relied entirely on the intense smoke produced during combustion to temporarily drive away mosquitoes. However, due to the pervasive smoke that irritated the nasal passages, and the fact that sulfur and wood shavings both contained slight toxins, they posed a significant health hazard. Moreover, because of their intense heat, carelessness often led to fires. Therefore, some hygiene-conscious individuals preferred to forgo their use and endure the harassment of mosquitoes.

Since the influx of Japanese-made "Pig Brand Anju" mosquito coils into our country, people found their manufacturing method novel and their effectiveness remarkable. Naturally, the superior prevailed over the inferior, and everyone abandoned the old for the new, rushing to purchase them. Domestically produced mosquito coils were defeated, and foreign mosquito coils flooded the Chinese market, resulting in an annual outflow of over one million yuan for our country.

The manufacturing of new-style mosquito coils uses white pyrethrum powder as the main raw material. Pyrethrum is a herbaceous plant that can be rotated with rice, wheat, and beans. It is also extremely easy to cultivate and can be planted on hillsides, in fields, in orchards, and in vegetable gardens, all with great success. Therefore, in countries like the United States, Australia, and Japan, pyrethrum occupies a significant part of agricultural production. The United States has the largest export volume. According to a 1928

survey, dry pyrethrum flowers alone amounted to over 9 million catties, valued at over 6 million yuan. Australia and Japan also produce a substantial amount. In recent years, Japan's export volume has been increasing annually. In 1910, Japan's dry pyrethrum flower export volume was only over 130,000 catties. Through twenty years of dedicated cultivation and vigorous promotion, it reached over 8.3 million catties by 1929. Such a rapid advancement has almost overwhelmed the United States and Australia in the world market and become the leader in the world. (To be continued)

Interview Record 193

— Zhujun

Here, we must state in advance: this is not an unconscious compliment, nor is it an advertisement for anyone. We feel that such a "foreign-educated doctor" is not easy to find in Chinese society. Although he does not boast of being a "big shot," people generally respect him as "China's Gandhi." This time, when Dr. Tai came south, this reporter had the opportunity to interview him. Now, the general content of the conversation is written out to introduce him to the people of the country and to inform those who aspire to promote national products. The reporter asked: "Promoting national products is indeed a matter of urgent importance, but it has been ineffective for decades. What is the reason?"

Dr. Tai replied: "This question is too broad in scope. In general,"

everyone is driven by the desire for beauty and the improvement of material life, and there is no effective organization in society for promoting national products and revitalizing industries. Furthermore, domestic products themselves often remain stagnant, so "promotion" after "promotion" has never been effective."

"Then what remedial measures does the doctor have for this?"

"For more than ten years, I have consistently advocated starting from each individual! Gradually extending to the general public, the most practical method is, of course, only personal thrift, which is what is called social thrift." Once we all stop using foreign goods, the tens of millions of dollars that go out every year can naturally be recovered. After recovering them, what should we do? We should come together to establish urban factories, rural cooperatives, etc., so that workers have food to eat and farmers have money to use, and then engage in production, selling the products throughout the country. This is what is called 'social production.' In short, these two

things are easy to do, but everyone just doesn't pay attention to them! "

Due to space constraints, many unimportant words cannot be written out one by one, but even this is very worthy of our attention.

Dr. Tai is only thirty-five or six years old, different from Lu Zuofu, the Gandhi of Sichuan. He is tall and sturdy, wearing a blue twill homespun worker's uniform, a duckbill cap, which he says is only worth one and a half cents, and black homespun shoes. His demeanor is gentle, his speech and laughter are kind, and he is thrifty and hardworking in everything. No one would know that he is a doctor from "Columbia" University!

Visiting Record

Going to the Countryside to Promote National Products 194

— Sun Licheng

The mosquito repellent incense used in our country in the old days was made of white paper circles, filled with wood chips containing toxic substances. Not only was the thick smoke irritating to the nose and harmful to health, but after burning, all the utensils in the room would change color, so families above the middle class

did not buy them. The mosquito repellent incense sold on the market now uses pyrethrum as the main raw material, supplemented with other fragrances. It is safe and effective, a wonderful product for boudoirs. Unfortunately, pyrethrum is cultivated very little in our country, and most of it has to be purchased from abroad, especially from Japan. As a result, the rights and interests are leaking out, which is not a small amount. The "Samsung Brand" mosquito repellent incense produced by the China Chemical Industry Society has a wide sales network. Recognizing that relying on other countries for raw materials is not a long-term solution, they have established pyrethrum gardens next to the Wusong River and Anlangdu in this city to promote cultivation. The other day, in order to arouse the interest of those who are interested in studying agriculture, the society invited people from all walks of life to visit the chrysanthemum garden. I also joined in and will briefly describe what I saw below. I believe that it will also be welcomed by enthusiastic comrades who promote national products.

At eight o'clock in the morning of that day, we gathered at the society's headquarters on Henan Road, and then rode in sixty Xiang Sheng Company cars, lined up on Aiyia Road. Each car was inserted with a small triangular flag. In addition to the Samsung trademark, the flag also printed the words "Go to the Countryside." After a while, the mighty force sped westward, passing Yuyuan Road, crossing the railway, passing Bili South Road, and getting off at Beixinjing, walking to Anlangdu, a total of more than 400 people. Everyone held paper fans given by the society to ward off the sun. The villagers along the way suddenly saw this large group of people going to the countryside, and they were all surprised. Old people and children leaned at the door and watched from afar. Some mistakenly thought they were going to the countryside to eat wedding banquets, and some thought they were coming to watch the games. The discussions were varied and innocent. The beans in the fields were withered and black, and the wheat was being harvested. Seeing plants more than a foot tall, with flowers like daffodils, everyone did not know what kind of plant it was. When asked the farmers, it was said that it was the "foreign mountain mushroom," which is used in big dishes. Everyone said that people in the city only know how to eat big dishes, but they don't know the foreign mountain mushroom, the raw material for big dishes, which is also a joke. After walking for three quarters of an hour, we arrived at the ferry. Looking at the flower garden from afar, the flowers were in full bloom, like a snow mountain, with a special flavor. Two ferries took turns ferrying people, which took a long time. Arriving at the chrysanthemum garden, there were more than a hundred farmers, with towels covering their heads and cloth bags hanging around their waists, picking flowers. It is said that each person can pick dozens of catties per day, and the labor cost per catty is 20 yuan. These are temporary short-term workers, because the second flower garden covers more than a hundred acres, and when the flowers are in bloom, the original workers are not enough to allocate. Hundreds of paces away from the flower garden, there are two five-bay thatched sheds (for drying and storing flowers) and a three-bay tile house (for workers to live in). The walls are covered with posters stating that the annual value of US pyrethrum dried flower exports is 7 million yuan and "planting pyrethrum to strive for self-sufficiency in raw materials, the purpose of which is to recover rights and interests," and other slogans. After eating Guanshengyuan refreshments in the thatched shed, we went to visit the flower garden. The reception staff explained in detail the cultivation method of pyrethrum, hoping that the visitors would imitate the planting, and that the society could buy the flowers harvested in the future at a good price, because the two chrysanthemum gardens, although they have hundreds of acres, the flowers harvested are not enough. At that time, the red sun was in the sky, and although everyone was sweating profusely, they were all in high spirits and not discouraged at all. Then the society distributed Yili public-use soda water. After drinking wildly, they felt that the scorching sun was not to be feared. The public relations doctor Huang Jingwan said that the experimental field for rural revitalization is centered on production and education, so he has a Chenggeng Work-Study Group near Huanghuacun in that area, and the China Chemical Industry Society's promotion of imitation of pyrethrum cultivation is the same purpose, and he is doing his best to persuade people to cooperate. Then a group photo was taken in the flower garden. When returning, everyone picked a few pyrethrum flowers, either worn on the chest or inserted on the hat, and everyone smiled. Arriving in Shanghai, it was already noon.

▲ Announcement: To Messrs. Tianran, Zhang Mengzhao, Rui Qisong, Qian, Yisheng, Liu Zengwei, Qin Shouou, Ke Ding'an, Shidian, Hu Louzhen, Guanshan, Quan, Manbin, Huang Jiafu, Zhenmu, Zhao Peng, Xu Nangong, Sun Choucheng, Jingcun, Zhu Shanxiu, Chen Jingyu, Guo Wei Songlu, Ziqiang, and Zhou Chengxun, your kind contributions in May are greatly appreciated. Please collect them from the accounting department of this office between 4:00 pm and 6:00 pm from the 6th to the 10th and the 16th to the 20th of this month, excluding Sundays.

Shen Bao National Products Weekly Editorial Department

Short Stories

Mr. Wang is Happy 195

— Liu Zengwei

Not far from Shanghai, there lived a Mr. Wang, who was about thirty years old. He had three sons, two daughters, and a wife, a family of seven, all of whom depended on his income as an accountant in a company. However, his income was very low, and since the place was not far from Shanghai, the atmosphere followed Shanghai. The modern ladies of Shanghai mostly liked to use foreign goods, so the middle and upper class people in that place also followed suit and used foreign goods extensively, resulting in a lot of expenses. Mr. Wang's family, although not considered an upper-class family, could be considered a middle-class family, so Mr. Wang's wife and children inevitably wanted to follow the trend and use foreign goods extensively, causing a lot of expenses and overspending. Mr. Wang repeatedly persuaded his family not to adopt the bad habits of the time, and that it would be better to wear homespun cloth and buy domestic goods. His wife and children were not willing to listen. Mr. Wang was so angry that his beard bristled, and he was so anxious that he could not think of a way. He frowned all day and night.

One day, Ah Lin saw Mr. Wang walking alone from afar, heading towards his place. He thought he was going to see his frowning face again. Unexpectedly, after getting closer and greeting him, he saw that Mr. Wang was very happy, with no trace of his previous worries. He was very surprised and could not help but ask what was going on. This question completely revealed the reason for Mr. Wang's happiness.

How did Mr. Wang become so happy? It turned out that through his own efforts, he had completely persuaded his family to use domestic goods. He had really considered it for a while. He thought that if his family was so superstitious about foreign goods, how could his meager income be enough for their expenses? If they continued to overspend year after year, the future consequences would be unimaginable, so he decided to take an opportunity to persuade them not to use foreign goods and to happily use domestic goods. He had just made up his mind when the China National Products Company held a national products fashion exhibition. He thought that he could take this opportunity to take his wife to see it, and perhaps he could change her mind about liking foreign clothing materials. So, when he had nothing to do at the company, he took his wife to visit the fashion exhibition. The result was very good. His wife said, "Domestic fashion is not worse than foreign clothing."

Some time later, the Ningbo Fellow Association held a national products promotion meeting. Mr. Wang thought that this was another good opportunity to persuade his family to like domestic goods. He took advantage of his free time to take his wife and children to participate in the promotion meeting. There were many people speaking at the promotion meeting, explaining the reasons for using domestic goods very thoroughly, and really hitting everyone's hearts. And everyone also swore to buy domestic goods. As a result, the influence on Mr. Wang's wife and children was indeed not small. They changed their minds from then on and no longer used foreign goods.

Since Mr. Wang's family stopped using foreign goods, the national products markets of the city's chamber of commerce and other national products companies often had the traces of Mrs. Wang and his children. But Mr. Wang's economy was much more relaxed. In the past, his monthly salary was never enough for expenses. Now, not only is it very generous every month, but there is also a surplus, because domestic goods are generally cheaper than foreign goods, and they are mostly durable. The styles may not be very good, but this is not important, and practicality is true. Moreover, the manufacturers of domestic goods are now studying improvement.

Once Mr. Wang's economy was relaxed, his frowning face disappeared, so Ah Lin, who had not seen him for several months, saw that Mr. Wang was very happy that day, and Mr. Wang was also very happy to tell him the reason for his happiness.

Spring and Autumn

The Smiling Tiger's Goodwill Diplomacy 196

— Qinglu

More than twenty people went hiking together. With a gust of bloody wind, a short-legged tiger jumped out of the mountain hollow, baring its fangs, ready to bite people.

If these people all had weapons for self-defense, then it would be more than enough for twenty people to subdue a fierce tiger. Unfortunately, they were all hiking unarmed, and their internal organization was lax, unable to punish the insult in unison. As a result, this tiger, relying on its sharp claws and teeth, wantonly ravaged this group of defenseless people! As a result, four of the twenty people were swallowed by it. According to the tiger's greed, it would be best to eat these twenty people all up, so that none would escape from the tiger's mouth. But, its heart was willing but its stomach was weak. Eating four people was already filling it up, and it had to digest for a while before it could move its appetite again.

Therefore, the tiger stretched its waist, put away its vicious attitude, and became a smiling tiger, saying to those who survived the tiger's mouth: "Dear ones, from now on, I won't eat you anymore. I want to transform the doctrine of eating people into goodwill diplomacy. Dear ones, don't be afraid."

Among the many survivors, one person said to the tiger: "Don't just be good in words. If you really want to show goodwill, why don't you spit out the four people you ate? Even if you can't spit them all out, you can spit out half. Returning our bones after eating our flesh is much better than empty words of goodwill, isn't it?"

The smiling tiger sneered: "Fool, do you think I'm really kind? The 'kin' I'm talking about is the 'kin' of King Tiger robbing a bride. The 'good' I'm talking about is the 'good' of a robber having a good heart."

The Main Gate Stands Wide Open 197

— Hualing

"The main gate stands wide open, those without money should not enter." This is how people in ancient times described the officials who only saw money. If you didn't spend white, flowery silver ingots, you shouldn't come to sue or file a lawsuit. Therefore, whenever the upright officials returned to the yamen, there were often aggrieved plaintiffs who bumped their heads on the street, blocking the sedan chair to file a complaint, crying and sniveling to cry out their grievances.

In ancient times, only the yamen had its main gate standing wide open, forbidding entry to the penniless. But now, in this year of 1933, it's no longer the case. No matter what place it is, the main gate stands wide open, forbidding entry to those without money.

Just look, with a school every five steps and a university every ten steps, which one doesn't have its main gate standing wide open? But the fees for tuition, food, lodging, books, servants, sports, library, and school construction, when calculated on the abacus, multiplying and dividing, will surely scare the fathers and brothers who earn a penny with a drop of sweat so much that they stick out their tongues and can't retract them.

The banks that have built 18-story buildings have their main gates standing wide open, but the poor laborers are only qualified to stand outside the wide-open gates and stare blankly for a while. Ordinary stores, although they have the words "Welcome to visit" written on their wide-open doors, if you, sir, have no "bills of exchange" and are just wandering around inside endlessly, the salesperson, afraid that you might steal something, will follow you step by step, "extremely sincere in their hospitality," making you feel embarrassed yourself.

Restaurants, hotels, theaters, dance halls, gambling dens, and brothels, without seven qian, one fen and five li, don't even think about walking into the wide-open gates. Even the compassionate old monks in the ancient temples in the forests, if they are holding a donation book, and you, sir, are blushing, your hand reaching into your pocket but unable to pull it out, that "kindly face" will surely make you pass the wide-open gates three times without daring to enter.

The pawnshop doors that stand wide open are said to be convenient for the poor. But a friend who doesn't even have a piece of foot cloth, even if they just want to admire the face of the pawnbroker, might feel a little cumbersome.

Scattered Strings 198

— Ye Yi Yi

A lawyer said, "Villagers file lawsuits mostly because of land disputes, and city dwellers file lawsuits always because of debt disputes"!

After finishing work, having no other trivial matters to pester you is the happiest time for a person.

If he is a cunning person, then don't pay attention to him. Smiling at him kindly is the most ferocious thing to do.

Many female students, in order to make their hair curly, go to the school doctor's office to ask for alcohol to perm it.

The lecture notes used in school, after a period of time, will be used to wrap things for you in the shops near the school.

Many smart friends are very sloppy.

A diligent friend may not have a good future, but a friend who can brag and flatter and is actually mediocre may have a lot of hope.

Women are like monkeys, good at imitation. When they see fashionable clothes, they will be thinking about them in their minds early on.

Wu Ziyu, Who Hides His Light in the Ancient Capital 199

— Zheng Yimei

General Wu Ziyu of Penglai has recently been living in seclusion in Shijin Garden in the ancient capital, dissipating his heroic spirit and deeply hiding his light. When newspaper reporters go to visit him, the gatekeeper always declines them, saying that the master is ill and cannot see guests. In fact, Wu spends his days planting flowers, raising fish, writing bamboo, chanting scriptures, and studying on his own. There is absolutely nothing wrong with his physical health. There is a type of green camellia in the garden, which Wu especially likes to admire. The camellia flower blooms white as snow, which is why Yang Wanli has the line "scattered fragrance snow blows on the railing," and Yuan Haowen has the line "jade tassels lie in the remnants of spring." It is rarely seen in crimson red. And since there is no bamboo in the north, Wu is even more diligent in painting bamboo, so that the verdant shadows of bamboo are always left between the brush and ink, compensating for what nature has not provided. When Lodong was tense, there were rumors outside that he had considerable contact with the Japanese and was about to be active in North China. Wu was very angry when he heard this, saying: In this time of national crisis, Wu has not been able to wield his hundreds of thousands of troops and sharpen his swords to repay the country, and his heart is deeply ashamed. How could he bear to take actions that betray the country and leave himself open to the contempt of the people? Some say that Wu is a person of extremely stubborn nature and is inherently disgusted with the Japanese. In the past, during the Fengzhi War, Wu led hundreds of thousands of brave and fierce soldiers from Sizhao Hall to Yuguan. The grandeur of the army, the abundance of vehicles, horses, guns, and equipment, the soaring momentum, and the earth-shattering sound were very pleasing to Wu. He invited observers from various countries, promising to report the war situation to foreign countries. However, the bottom draft of the report had to be reviewed by Wu before it could be telegraphed, so as to avoid the leakage of secrets. Unexpectedly, Japanese newspapers often published secret messages from Wu's army. Wu was greatly surprised and ordered a search of the observers' trains. He found twelve military pigeons in the Japanese train, which were the source of the secret messages. Wu was furious and immediately executed the twelve pigeons, grinding his teeth and saying: The Japanese are cunning and will surely harm me in the future. Killing the pigeons is to show my determination to eliminate cunning and eradicate deception. This happened in the thirteenth year of the Republic of China. The words are still in my ears, so it can be known that the rumors in the past are absolutely not true. I deeply hope that Wu will take good care of himself, for there is still a day to protect the country.

Wheelbarrow 200

— You Qi

The time has come again. From that towering and majestic chimney, there is a long and loud roar that is full of arrogance. Following that, as usual, a large crowd of people squeezed out like a tidal wave.

Here, there is no regulation on age, ranging from seven or eight years old to thirty or forty years old. At the same time, there is no regulation on the province of origin. Whether it is Jiangbei, Jiangnan, or people from other provinces, they are all within the "logic." The so-called logic is not that anyone can be "logged" and then "edited." Those who have not gone through a certain stage are also just "staring blankly." Although they have different ages, they have the same line in the haggard expression shown by the long hours of work. Is it intentional "forced smiles" or an expression of "sincere feelings"? They are talking and laughing with each other, even arguing, and striding in messy steps on the bumpy stone road.

The groups of waiters rub their eyes, which they think are blurred, and shoot out greedy light, rotating and sweeping. The tense expression is revealed in everyone's eyebrows, as if they want to capture something, or as if they want to discover something.

The wheelbarrows that have gathered from nowhere are neatly arranged in formation, waiting for the soldiers and generals flashing out from the "banners and flags."

Sure enough, after no more than two "rounds," they were finally captured, disappearing into the glow of the setting sun under the triumphant harmony of the "creaking" sounds.

No hot summer, no cold winter. Day after day, wheelbarrows gather from all directions and return in triumph.

Northeast Four Company Commanders 201

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Eight: Indignant Words Prompt Youth to Resign and Retreat

Warm Hearted Compassion Shown as Maiden Brings Padded Clothing

At this time, Gui Zhi was indeed paying attention to Ji Zhi's actions, thinking that she had stimulated him with those harsh words the other day, and he should have some kind of response. So she waited quietly for two days to see how things would turn out. Unexpectedly, she waited a whole week without seeing any news. Helpless, she had to use the same method as before to inquire about his whereabouts from the maid of the Gan family. According to the maid, one day, the second master packed up his bedding and luggage and left the yamen. It seemed like he was angry with the master, but the master didn't say anything to him at home. According to our mistress, the master recommended him to the city, and he has got a good job. Gui Zhi asked, "Which day did he leave?" The maid said, "It seems to be the day of the Lantern Festival. We ate Yuanxiao that day, and there was one person missing in the family." Gui Zhi thought, it was indeed on the Lantern Festival that she used words to stimulate him. Unexpectedly, he left that day. This clearly shows that he is avoiding me further. Thinking this way, she didn't need to inquire any further and went straight home. This time, just like the last time she heard the news from the old nanny, she couldn't wait to close the door and cry bitterly. However, her mother was doing work in the room and wouldn't allow her to cry again, so she lay on the tea table outside, pretending to doze off, and tried her best to hold back her tears. Seeing this situation in the room, Jiang Shi guessed that she had committed something to her heart again, and thought to herself that she might as well take this opportunity to make a final effort to explore her tone. She said: "Old girl, bring in the two pairs of thread socks that are drying on the rope. Those are all for Company Commander Zhao. I have to sew them for him." Gui Zhi didn't say anything, brought in two pairs of socks, and threw them on the kang. Jiang Shi said: "Do I have to do this little thing? Just find two pieces of cloth and sew the soles for Company Commander Zhao." Gui Zhi took the socks in her hand and looked at them, and said: "The bottom of the socks is not broken, why add a good bottom?" Jiang Shi said: "You don't know, Company Commander Zhao is a man who knows how to live. He knows that it is always difficult for shoes and socks to be on the drill field every day, so hurry up and make up the soles first. In my opinion, this person is good in every way." Gui Zhi didn't say anything, pulled out a drawer in the broken wooden closet, rummaged in it for a while, found two pieces of cloth, and started to mend the soles of the socks on the kang (93)

[L> Miscellaneous Remarks

Choosing a Wife 202

— Heng Qiu

丨Analysis of Types of Women丨

All those who are unwilling to be monks have a lifelong event丨marriage丨waiting for you to solve. Why did the ancients regard the two words marriage as a major event? Simply put, it is to tell you not to treat it as a trivial matter that is easy to solve! But now the general youth, when the opportunity is rare, see a woman and try their best to attack her; often before they have any understanding of her nature, they have already developed feelings for her. Once there are feelings between men and women, all reason is destroyed. How dangerous is this? Therefore, it has created divorce, abandonment, remarriage∶∶∶all kinds of marital sins.

All those who are unwilling to be monks must marry a wife. To marry a wife, you must be careful. To be careful, you must make a careful selection of each of the people you know. But before the big selection, we must understand what kinds of women there are in society? After several meticulous analyses, I have about five types:

(1) Rural women who can support themselves

She is a wildflower by the roadside, with a natural beauty that is always revealed, and a natural force to feed herself; she does not need artificial irrigation, nor will she emit a strong fragrance to attract people's attention.

(2) Small family women who take marrying a husband as a profession

Their motto is: "Rely on parents at home, rely on husband after marriage." Their only responsibility after marriage is to pass on the family line for their husband. Most of them are very obedient and admit that they are appendages of men.

(3) Daughters of wealthy families who regard their husbands as slaves

They are the proud children of heaven, and they often want to find a gentle and considerate husband to be their personal slave. Therefore, they like to discuss and study the method of "how to make their husbands succumb" the most, because they have a lot of money, and the law can protect them very well, so they are not afraid of their husbands divorcing them.

(4) Romantic women who regard men as playthings

They can use artificial colors to anesthetize men, and they can use perfume and lipstick to exchange for a beautiful life. Most of them are social butterflies, dancers, actors, and others who make a living by their appearance. Their magic power is: they can overturn your reason, they can transfer your joys and sorrows, and they can manipulate your entire life in their hands. But when they encounter powerful people, they themselves will become men's playthings.

(5) Modern girls with considerable knowledge

Most of them are school teachers, company employees, and red flower vases in government agencies. They all have considerable knowledge. Because they can be independent, they all think they are the most modern women. They look down on any kind of women. Their eyes seem to be born on their foreheads, which can be said to be extremely arrogant. Therefore, it is not easy to be their husbands. Unless they have more knowledge, wealth, and status than them, they can never escape their contempt.

Because there are also many kinds of men, I don't need to determine which kind of woman is the best. I just need to: clarify the types of women before starting the first step of choosing a wife 丨 determine which kind of woman is most suitable for your own environment, 丨 after determining, start to find a woman among the types you have determined whose personality, knowledge, and appearance are suitable for you to be a wife (as to whether she thinks you are suitable or not is another question), then you can always get a really happy result.

Many young people do not have enough common sense in choosing a wife, and they only pay attention to small goals, thinking that as long as the personality, knowledge, and appearance are suitable, it is enough, but they do not know the importance of the big goal 丨 analyzing the types of women 丨, thus causing all kinds of marital tragedies. Because her personality, knowledge, and appearance, although you think they have passed, when her status and environment do not match you, you will get unexpected disappointment. Young people! Young people who are unwilling to be monks! Be careful of your major events

The slaughter and tooth tax of the Jiangsu education fund, which is more than one million, accounts for about one-third of the education expenses of the entire province. Wuhan Construction Funds Still Allocated as Before 208

The construction funds for the new campus of Wuhan University were temporarily suspended due to some reason. Now it is heard that the school has received a letter from the Ministry of Finance stating that the monthly construction fee of 20,000 yuan will still be allocated as before. In the future, the monthly regular construction fees will total 85,000 yuan, which is the same as the amount received in the past. The school has many formal matters to complete in the future. If the construction funds can continue to be allocated, the progress will be easier.

▲Qian Jiazhi and other five people serve as standing committee members of the examination committee

The Zhejiang Provincial Education Department is actively preparing for the high school graduation examination for the second semester of the 21st year. Each committee member identified the subjects for which they would be the chief examiner as follows: Dai Jingshan (Chinese), Chen Shuliang (History), Wu Dezhang (English), Xue Yuanhe (Physics), Shen Yanghou (Chemistry), Wang Gui, Rong (Mathematics), Hu Jianzhong (Party Principles), Xue Dexi (Biology), Zhang Qixun (Geography). 3. The assistant examiners for each subject, four to five people per subject, are recommended by the chief examiner and determined before June 10. 4. The staff handling the examination are appointed by the chairman of the committee. 5. The examination instructions were revised and passed. 6. The examination room rules were revised and passed. 7. The procedures for reviewing the qualifications of candidates were passed. 8. The standards for remediation and grade retention were revised and passed. 9. The detailed rules for the operation of the examination offices in each district were handed over to the standing committee for supplementary revision and then submitted to the chairman of the committee for approval.

Local

City Education Association's Measures for Fundraising for Education 212

The Shanghai City Education Association launched the one yuan per month education movement, and hired many economic committee members to form an economic committee to raise funds separately. The fundraising methods are recorded as follows: (1) The one yuan per month education fund is raised by the economic committee members. (2) Donations are divided into two types, A and B. Type A is for those who pay in one lump sum, and Type B is for those who pay monthly. The City Education Association will issue receipts separately for both types. (3) The minimum donation is one yuan. Those who recognize Type B donations must donate continuously for at least four months (because continuous donations for four months can cultivate students to graduation). (4) Those who donate 200 yuan in Type A or donate 50 yuan per month in Type B will use the name of the donor as the name of a certain grade. Those who donate 400 yuan in Type A or donate 100 yuan per month in Type B will use the name of the donor as the name of a certain school, so that the students of that grade school will remember the source of their drinking water to commemorate it. (5) Those who donate more than 1,000 yuan in Type A or donate more than 250 yuan per month in Type B, in addition to handling matters in accordance with the previous paragraph, will also be requested by the主管官署to reward them according to law. (6) Donations will be temporarily deposited in the Shanghai Bank, and two people will be appointed by the Education Association from among the economic committee members to keep them together. (7) The verification of the funds will be handled by the Board of Supervisors of the City Education Association. (8) These measures will be implemented after being approved by the City Education Association.

Christian Primary Schools in this City Hold Labor Education Discussion Meeting 213

▲Handicraft Achievement Exhibition is Open to the Public

The Shanghai Christian Primary School Teacher Discussion Meeting convened by the China East China Christian Education Association at No. 23 Yuanmingyuan Road in this city started on time at 2:00 pm on the 6th at the Moore Church on Xizang Road. The general theme of this discussion is "How to Train Children's Manual Labor to Work Effectively." The association specially invited Mr. An Daling, a professor at Guanghua University, to give a lecture on "The Implementation of Labor Education." He gave a detailed explanation of the objects, purposes, teaching materials, and future of labor education. Before the lecture, there was a song from the Russian Children's Choir. At 3:30, an achievement exhibition was held, including woodworking, carving, earthwork, bamboo work, embroidery, sewing, etc. At 4:20, a manual education discussion meeting was held, presided over by Chen Heqin, the director of the Chinese Education Department of the工部局. Representatives from various schools fully provided their opinions and discussed with each other. At 6:00, all members had a meal together, and at 7:00, an educational film was shown. The meeting adjourned at 8:00. It was found that 18 schools including Juemin Primary School, Qingxin Primary School, McLaren Primary School, and Biwen Primary School participated in this meeting, with a total of more than 120 representatives. In addition, the association's handicraft achievement exhibition will be fully open from 9:00 am to 5:00 pm every day before this Thursday. Schools that want to visit can contact the Moore Church office.

University Education Associations Host University and Middle School Debate Competitions 219

▲To be held during the Academic Salvation Movement Week

The Academic Research Association of the Shanghai University Faculty and Staff Union, to enhance students' language skills, train logical thinking methods, and stimulate their interest in academic research, is hosting Chinese and English debate competitions for major universities and middle schools in East China. The competitions are scheduled to take place during the Academic Salvation Movement Week. Each university, independent college, specialized school, and middle school in the Beijing-Shanghai-Suzhou-Hangzhou area can send one Chinese and one English debate team. Each team should consist of two debaters. The topic for the Chinese debate is "China should immediately establish an educational and cultural bank," and the topic for the English debate is "Chinese universities should only offer four departments in the future: agriculture, engineering, medicine, and science." Each school's debate teams will be divided into pro and con groups, and will be eliminated in sequence during the competition to produce the final winning pro and con groups. The order of debates will be determined by drawing lots. The association has raised prize money from the banking sector to reward the winners of each group.

Great China Middle School Adds School Buildings 222

The Great China Middle School on Zhongshan Road currently has 698 male and female students and 71 faculty and staff members. The teaching facilities are known to be perfect. However, because the university also holds classes in the Qunxian Hall of the school, it feels crowded. Therefore, it was decided to add a school building. The number of rooms required has been determined to be 18 ordinary classrooms, 4 special classrooms, and 8 director's offices, achievement rooms, etc., which can accommodate 1,000 students for teaching and office use. The drawings have been submitted and it is expected to be completed around the Double Tenth Festival this year. In addition, the school's 8th summer school session will begin on July 7th and end on August 20th. A brochure is available and will be sent immediately upon request.

Municipal Xinlu Normal School Students' Practice Teaching 223

Students from the Municipal Xinlu Normal School's senior normal and rural normal programs are about to graduate. Before graduation, they are required to have a long period of practice teaching. Currently, because the school has few affiliated primary school grades and in order to increase students' teaching and guidance experience, it has been approved by the Municipal Education Bureau to use the Municipal Wanzhu, Xicheng, Shishihua, Yangzheng, Gaochang, Yongning, and Duchuan primary schools, which are relatively large and well-known, as practice teaching schools. It is learned that the school has already begun practice teaching with 65 students, divided into 15 groups, responsible for teaching various subjects and various guidance matters. Last Friday, the first large-scale practice teaching was held at Xicheng Primary School.

Next Olympic Games Approved to be Held in Berlin 226

Should not be subject to any hindrance

(National News Agency, Vienna, 7th) The Olympic Congress opened here today with solemn ceremony. Mikleres, Chairman of the International Olympic Committee and Chairman of the Austrian Committee, delivered a speech declaring that the 1936 Olympic Games should still be held in Berlin, saying that it is not only the desire of the whole world, but also for the benefit of the whole world, and that the holding of the Olympic Games should not be subject to any hindrance. The meeting then passed this proposal.

Philippines Actively Building Far Eastern Games Venue 227

▲Athletic field in Manila's Lira Ditiro

▲Large swimming pool under construction

▲Basketball at Santo Tomas University court

▲Baseball and volleyball courts to be completed before the Games

(Manila Special Dispatch) With only one year left before the 10th Far Eastern Games, the Philippine sports community is extremely tense about the preparations for the Games. The Philippine Sports Association is now cooperating with the Manila Municipal Authority to transform the city's existing Lira Ditiro sports field for use as the athletic field for the next Far Eastern Games. The renovation project has been completed, and its scope is no less than that of the Meiji Jingu Athletic Field of the previous Games. In addition, a large swimming pool is being built near the field, which is currently under construction. The pool is 50 meters long and 20 meters wide, and the viewing stand can accommodate 5,000 people. The basketball court will be located at the basketball court of Santo Tomas University. The court is great, with seating for 5,000 around it, so no special construction is required. As for the baseball and volleyball courts, a suitable location has not yet been selected, but it is expected to be completed before the opening of the Games. If necessary, it will be located inside the athletic field. The soccer field is attached to the center of the athletic field, and the tennis courts are already well-equipped tennis courts used by the carnival.
