The Burst of Freedom 240

— Qi Fan

The cry for freedom is present in every era. I, however, said last time, "Do not want freedom," as if deliberately trying to be strange. But freedom must have limits, must have scope, isn't this what people often say? And most people recognize these words. Freedom that has scope and limits, can it still be freedom? Then, it is better not to have freedom at all.

The struggle for freedom often arises between groups and individuals. Groups often want to limit individual freedom, interfere with individual freedom, and deny individual freedom. If an individual is a member of a group, if he understands that he belongs to the group, he will always be willing not to have freedom, and allow the will of the group to dominate. Because individuals and groups cannot be opposed, the status of the group is higher than the individual, and the group has absolute dominance.

The composition of a group is based on the common and consistent interests of that group. Therefore, the interests of the group are the interests of all the members of the group. The group's absolute power of dominance is based on this point. However, when the organization of a group becomes ill, so that it cannot represent the common interests of a group, each individual feels dissatisfied with the dominance of the group, and the cry for freedom is then issued.

For example, the state was originally organized for the welfare of all the people, and the people always obey the central government and support the government. But when the people realize that a national government is only an institution for collecting taxes, exploiting, and oppressing, the people have a cry for freedom. All the facilities of the state, not taking the welfare of the people as a prerequisite, have already lost the original purpose of the group organization, that is, they have become ill, so there is this discovery of the disease.

The cry for freedom is really a symptom of disease. A clever ruler knows that a disease must be treated, while a stupid one is often very stupid, does not recognize that it is a disease, treats the power of the group as divinely ordained, and does not see the common interests in the fundamental place, and wants to abuse that power to suppress. Then, they will get to the point where it cannot be cleaned up. These fools do not understand the meaning of the group, nor do they understand the basis of power. They rashly engage in politics, which is as dangerous as a blind man driving a car.

Those who feel alarmed by the cry for freedom are still capable of being made. Only stupid people persistently adopt high-pressure policies, and as a result, they will inevitably trigger an explosion of freedom.

Talking About the Eleventh Art 241

— Li Jinming

When you reach a certain age, entertainment becomes boring. I remember ten years ago, because I felt that I was not a Philistine, I wanted to get involved in anything new, especially movies. Later, my experience of the world gradually changed, and I felt that what movies love to show is not very believable, so I didn't think about it for five or six years. But I didn't know that in these five or six years, movies have made remarkable progress. In terms of both content and technique, they sometimes surpass many great literary works. (Thought cannot be discussed!)

I think that the reason why movies have become an art, and movie stars have become the eleventh muse, is mostly due to the director. In the four films—"Kurier", "The Big House", "Morocco", "Grand Hotel"—I not only saw the directors' ability to manipulate the acting talent of the stars, but also their ability to choose excellent literary themes, and their ability to find some formulas in aesthetic methods, to turn plain impressions into strong impressions, and to turn a plate of bean sprouts into the flavor of curry chicken.

Although "Kurier" is a romance, there is not a single slack spot from beginning to end—the best thing is its contrast (these are all terms in aesthetics and rhetoric). As the saying goes, sorrow is seen through joy—this is originally the principle of drama, and it can be seen in Shakespeare's Romeo and Juliet, where there are jokes. In Chinese old dramas, a play of "Si Lang Visits His Mother" must be followed by a play of "The In-Laws Enter the City to Collect Additional Taxes", which is also this kind of gimmick, but it depends on whether you compare it accurately or not. To put it bluntly, "Kurier" is completely classical; clearly you feel that this kind of thing will not happen, but after watching it, it has to make you believe it.

"The Big House" and "Grand Hotel" are completely realistic, while "Morocco" is realistic and has a symbolic flavor. Some people say that "The Big House" is also symbolic; Wallace Berry's thug represents the revolution, and Louis Stone's prison guard represents the reaction. As a result, the reaction leveled the revolution, and it seemed to say that under the red light, the royalist thoughts of Mussolini and Hitler came out. In art, it is not necessarily something that cannot be written about. However, this kind of explanation, in my opinion, is like professors researching "Dream of the Red Chamber", not necessarily reliable; it is inevitable that it is completely realistic, as long as the audience can experience some prison life. The most touching thing is the revival of Christian thought inside.

"Morocco" is simply an epitome of the life of a fugitive lair. Marlene Dietrich's success is truly amazing. (In my opinion, she is ten times better than Garbo.) Intrigue, insidiousness, assassination, fate, and revenge—in this composition, the heroes and beauties that are born really have nothing that makes people think it is artificial. The ending still says: Love, go to the desert! This is like saying: The bluebird exists, but it cannot be kept in a cage. . . . Comparing "Grand Hotel" to "The Big House" and "Morocco" is like comparing naturalism to realism; the content is not tense, and under the light performance, you see life and death, tragedy and comedy in urban life, and it seems to carry some lessons on how to be a human being.

If China could produce this kind of film, and even if it is subject to all kinds of restrictions, it would not necessarily be glorious.

Ah Lin 242

— Peng Xuezhen

Late at night, I emerged alone from Lin Niu's house, securing the broken door, and strolled along the street filled with the whispering June evening breeze.

Just three days ago, Lin was speaking with joy and hope, still supporting her faltering steps to come and go, her face always adorned with a smile. What happened now, that she lies stiffly there, with white wax candles lit at her head!

I gazed at the pair of newborn children lying on Lin's bed, their cheeks flushed with the unique redness of infants, their little eyes closed in slumber. These two ignorant children do not yet know that their mother has left this human world forever, just as they have stepped into this world of light, just as they have opened their slender little eyes.

In the crying of the children is buried the robust life of the young mother, although the children cry because of unease or fear of the new world, Lin gazes at her elderly mother standing before the bed, gazes at the many people around her, known or unknown, and writhing her entire body, begins her journey to another world. Perhaps this journey is eternal, filled with fresh experiences.

Lin was a woman of candid heart. The face tanned by labor under the sun could never hide her healthy skin. She did not speak much, but every word was sincere, convincing to the listener. Every day she would rise so early in the morning to wash clothes, the clear water flowing under the bridge, Lin barefoot, squatting by the riverbank, every strike of the wooden club imbued with the life of her and her mother. Every afternoon they would go to various places to collect clothes, using their hands, plus water and sunlight besides the soap, they truly lived in the gifts of nature.

But one day, Lin suddenly disappeared. It was said that she had left with a man. The old mother, squinting her eyes, told people that her daughter had gone to another city to enjoy good fortune.

"You see, soon Lin and her son-in-law will come to pick me up, and we will no longer suffer, washing clothes, winter is truly bitter." The old woman smiled mysteriously, but the busybodies did not quite believe her words, making wild guesses.

The days flowed away like the water under the bridge, never to return.

Just as when she had left, one day, Lin suddenly quietly slipped back, wearing clothes she had never had before, her eyes appearing sunken, often lost in thought, no longer as lively as before, the old woman no longer smiled and laughed in front of people.

Lin deteriorated further, washing clothes listlessly on the river beach every day, sometimes gazing silently at the river for a long time, returning home with a bitter expression.

No one knew Lin's secret, and no one knew the sorrow in her heart. People simply sighed inexplicably for this girl.

Lin's belly grew bigger day by day.

Childishly, Lin shyly sewed clothes for her future child under the sun, a smile revealing the joy of motherhood, but that joy contained a deep-seated resentment.

Now, Lin has passed away with her secrets and sorrow. Isn't it the dead Lin lying there today? In the sea of life, a bubble has dissolved, carried away by a wave.

Like a ghost, I walked eastward, the river surging as if sobbing, and in the shadow of the ancient trees by the roadside, I felt Lin walking towards me, as lively as before, coming to our alley to collect clothes.

Children 243

— Su

For several days, I hadn't left my house because I wasn't feeling well; today, I went to see a doctor and took a walk outside.

The places I passed were still the narrow alleys, the sunless streets, and the dusty roads. In those places, I saw many children.

Groups of children gathered in the streets, jumping, running, shouting, and making noise; no one stopped them, and no one protected them. They ran wildly from street to street, as if the street was their only paradise.

In every patch of empty ground along the walls, there were several children tossing coins. They seemed very interested in this activity, staying there for a long time.

As I passed through a quiet alley, a child led a blind child past me; he kept his eyes tightly closed, one hand resting on the shoulder of the child in front, gently tapping a small stick, slowly traversing the secluded alley with his companion.

On the road: three bare-chested children dragged three strings of worn-out straw sandals, panting as they walked; a pre-pubescent rickshaw puller struggled to pull an empty cart, soliciting business from passersby; under the shade of a tree, a woman was feeding the baby in her arms, and standing beside her were several children, who, upon seeing someone approach, would follow behind them, singing: "Good sir, good master, please do a good deed!" extending their hands, hoping people would give them a third of a big pancake as the price.

In front of the garbage bins by the roadside, children scavenging through the trash were bent over, searching in the bins; scraps of torn cloth, empty tin cans, glass bottles, meat bones, chicken and duck feathers, these were all their treasures, which they carefully picked up and placed in their small baskets.

At the foot of the big bridge, two or three children were waiting; when a rickshaw crossed the bridge, they would race each other to push the rickshaw from behind, one hand pushing and the other hand extended, begging for money from the person riding in the rickshaw, whispering "Sir, sir," following them all the way from one side of the bridge to the other.

One of the passengers said, "There are so many children in the streets that they are crowded!"

Returning home, I opened the newspaper that had just arrived, and in one corner was published: "Two Students Simultaneously Missing

丨Will States They Will Enter the Mountains to Seek the Tao"

Ah! These children! Is there anyone who thinks about these children, who is willing to save these children?

Red Carrot Whiskers 244

— Translated by Lin, from Jules Renard

Spring Water (Continued)

Godfather丨Sleep, you beast, sleep!

But the godfather and godson could not fall asleep. Red Carrot Whiskers tossed and turned, suffocating, seeking air to breathe, which made his old godfather feel a little sorry for him.

Suddenly, just as Red Carrot Whiskers was about to fall asleep, the godfather grabbed his arm and said:

"Are you here, you beast? I'm dreaming, I feel like you're still in the spring water. Do you remember the time you fell into the spring water?"

Red Carrot Whiskers丨As clear as if I were still in there right now, Godfather. I don't blame you for it, but you often bring it up to me.

Godfather丨Poor beast, I shudder all over whenever I think about it. I was asleep on the grass then. You were playing by the spring water, you slipped, you fell into the spring water, you were shouting, you were struggling, and I, damn it all, didn't hear anything. The spring water wasn't very deep, only good enough to drown a cat, but you didn't stand up. That's where the trouble lies, didn't you think to stand up then?

Red Carrot Whiskers丨Do you think I can still remember what I was thinking when I was sinking into the spring water!

Godfather丨In the end, you making such a racket in the water finally woke me up. Luckily, you didn't drown. Poor beast! Poor beast! You were spitting like a water dragon. Someone changed your clothes for you, put you in Little Belna's Sunday clothes.

Red Carrot Whiskers丨That's right, those clothes made me itchy all over. I was scratching all over. It was practically a 　-lined garment.

Godfather丨No, it was because Little Belna didn't have a clean 　shirt to lend you. I'm laughing now, but back then, if it had been one more minute, no, one more second, you would have been dead.

Red Carrot Whiskers丨Then I would be far away from you now.

Godfather丨Don't say that. I'm even saying some stupid things. Since that mess happened, I haven't slept a good night. I suffer from insomnia, this is my punishment; I should be suffering this punishment.

Red Carrot Whiskers丨And me, Godfather, I shouldn't be suffering this punishment, I really want to fall asleep.

Godfather丨Sleep, you beast, sleep.

Red Carrot Whiskers丨If you want me to sleep, Godfather, then please loosen my hand. Let me sleep soundly before you grab me again. And please spread your legs apart too, because the hair on your legs is making me terribly itchy. I can't fall asleep no matter what when someone is touching me.

U.S. Cotton Bull Market Concludes 254

Yesterday, the U.S. cotton market experienced mixed conditions. Favorable weather and bull market profit-taking led to a decline. As a result, spot prices fell by 15 points per pound, and futures prices fell by 12 points per pound. The Liverpool cotton market saw no change in spot prices, while futures prices fell by 8 to 9 points. The Egyptian cotton market saw no change in spot prices. The Bombay cotton market initially rose following the U.S. market but then weakened due to bull market profit-taking. Consequently, Pingar rose by 3 rupees, while Omra and White Western both rose by 3.5 rupees. Original telegram on the left (dated June 6th).

Silk and Tea: Market Notes on Silk Cocoons 255

Chongde Cocoon Firm Closed: Chongde's cocoon production only reached 30-40% of previous levels, and the firm's receipts were insufficient. Weighing and transactions have now ceased, and the firm has closed. Cocoon prices reached a maximum of 45 yuan for foreign varieties and a minimum of 25 yuan for local varieties.

Changxing Cocoon Prices Relatively Stable: Cocoon firms are gradually ceasing weighing and transactions, with receipts only reaching 50%. The highest cocoon prices are for improved varieties, ranging from 40 to 45 yuan, while local varieties range from 26 to 32 yuan.

Dantu Foreign Varieties Show Little Shrinkage After Drying: Cocoon production is still abundant, and the cocoons are of relatively good quality. Firms are actively weighing and collecting, and the account books are quite lively. Cocoon prices reached a maximum of 50 yuan (for improved variety cocoons), with a drying shrinkage of only 280 catties. Local variety cocoons were priced at 32.3 yuan.

Changshu High-Quality Cocoons Expected to Rise: The number of silkworms raised this year has decreased. Although cocoon production is abundant, many cocoon firms have opened for business. Prices for improved variety cocoons are expected to rise. The initial opening price was 34-35 yuan, which then rose to 37-38 yuan. The current opening price is 40 yuan. The initial opening price for local variety cocoons was 25-26 yuan, which has now reached 30 yuan.

Nanjing Cocoon Reeling Shrinkage is Small: Improved varieties account for 70-80% of production. The cocoons are of relatively good quality. According to the results of trial reeling in Shanghai, the drying shrinkage of improved variety dry cocoons is only 450-460 catties (i.e., 100 catties of raw silk). High-quality local variety cocoons show 560-570 catties.

Changjiang (Yangtze) Trading Houses Continue to Import Artificial Silk: Sichuan, Hubei, and Hunan firms have declared imports of brands such as Golden Double Deer, Black Beauty, Golden Unicorn, and Paida Wu, etc. Forty-eight cases of futures for June and July were traded at prices ranging from 181.75 yuan to 172.25 yuan net.

Shanghai Silk Market Expects Rise in Prices; Holding Back: Yesterday, New York silk prices soared another 5 points, with the current silk price at US$1.80 per pound. Yokohama silk prices also rose sharply by 35 yen, with the price at 945 yen. Shanghai Chinese silk fell sharply but rebounded slightly. Yesterday, overseas yellow and white silk both had incoming orders, but the arrival prices only rose by 1.20 yuan. Sales were difficult due to heavy cost, and sentiment is bullish with the market holding back. Fifty bales of Lu factory silk and eighty bales of Shanghai White factory silk were transacted at a price increase of 20 yuan. Fifteen bales of Sichuan factory silk and three bales of coarse yellow silk were also priced firmly.

Tea Merchants From Various Regions Showing Slight Activity 256

Yesterday, in the Shanghai tea market, merchants from Yingzhuang, Jinlong, Yihe, and Xiehe, etc., began processing Zhenmei green tea from Wudong, Tunxi, Yin County, and other regions. The market showed slightly more activity. Needle-shaped Zhenmei was particularly popular, and prices were quite firm. Due to demand signaled by telegram from Bombay, merchants from Gaoli Zhuang Gongxi, Baitou Zhuang Qianyi, and Yulong, etc., in Wuyuan also began searching for green tea, which was slightly more stable than before. Although British merchants such as Tianxiang and Baochang, etc., started processing Qimen black tea, the volume was not large, and market prices were weak.

Grains: Rice Prices in Both Northern and Southern Markets Fall Frequently 257

(South Shanghai): Sources from more than 50 stores; both are sluggish, and the situation is dull. Changbang, Sujian Japonica, and Nangang thick rice prices are slightly lower by one or two jiao. Only high-quality rice is slightly fresher in color. Qingjiao, Songsi, Xilian, and other thin rice varieties from Jinping and Weisanbang continue to process one thousand several hundred packages, and the price also fell by two jiao. Du Yangjian follows Japonica rice by a small amount of jiao. The exchange is balanced. The market shows no significant gains or losses.

(North Shanghai): Eight or nine boats from the Hexia region. White rice sales are slow, the market is sluggish, and surrounding areas lack trade, causing prices to weaken. Thin rice is dull, and prices are slightly lower by a small margin. Early rice is down by one or two jiao. Yangdu has continuous arrivals, and sales are still acceptable, but prices are down by a few fen. Wharf customer Jianjiao is sluggish, and the exchange is flat and weak. Although there are few arrivals of Baiyuan, there is still stock in the river, and retail discounts are not working. Gao Dingzhong carries a weak tone.

Northern Merchants are Buying Saigon Rice 258

Yesterday, foreign merchants experienced divergent trends in rice prices. The stock of Xiang and Gan rice among the guest rice varieties is very sufficient, and sporadic small quantities continue to arrive at the port. However, sales rely solely on the Fuzhou group. Since the demand from Fuzhou has weakened, sentiment is soft, and merchants are mostly seeking to sell early. Although the Wenzhou group has sales, the volume is ultimately not as large as that of the Fujian group. Yesterday, the Wenzhou group only purchased Nanjing and Wuxi indica rice. Xiang and Gan rice are still purchased exclusively by Fujian merchants. Due to the weak market, transactions are more frequent by small margins. 2230 bags were sold, Nanjing and Wuxi machine-milled rice were at the Shanghai Railway Station Bureau, Nanjing machine-milled rice was at 7.57 yuan, Wuxi machine-milled rice was at 7.60 yuan, Jiangxi machine-milled late rice was at 8.35 yuan, Hunan secondary machine-milled oil rice was at 8.35 yuan, rough red rice was at 8.15 yuan, and rough Jing rice was at 6.90 yuan. Yesterday, the foreign rice market turned brisk due to inquiries from various regions, but there was not much high-quality rice on the market, and merchants uniformly raised prices. Foreign firms held back. Yesterday, Northern merchants purchased in the market, and the situation was particularly good. Subsequently, one lot of 700 bags of Saigon rice was sold, with the Northern merchants taking 500 bags and Fuzhou taking 200 bags, at a price of 8.45 yuan. This was a new shipment brought in by the Fuka Foreign Firm a month ago. Most of the market inventory is old rice, so the selling price was particularly good.

Lending of Wheat and Wheat Attacks on Trademarked Flour Wheat 259

The flour market has gradually weakened since opening this morning, with a downward trend and a bleak outlook. The closing prices were down by 0.025 yuan for November, down by 0.027 yuan each for June and October, down by 0.0175 yuan for July, down by 0.015 yuan for September, and down by 0.0125 yuan for August. There are many reasons for the market decline, the most important being the U.S. lending wheat in large amounts and the new wheat entering the market. The new wheat is good everywhere. Arrivals have been continuous in the Nanjing area, and other places should also see a consistent market within this ten-day period. Traders from the production areas are strongly disposing of goods in view of the situation of foreign wheat. Foreign wheat futures also fell by 0.02-0.03 yuan, and there is talk of a scheduled shipment of large quantities of borrowed wheat, so hoarding and reselling, speculation, and cautious sales are prevailing, and factory dumping is particularly intense. The market is falling again and again and cannot be sustained.

The wheat market continues to decline because foreign wheat telegrams are down by 0.02-0.03 yuan. Borrowed wheat is scheduled to arrive in China, and new and old wheat are gradually arriving in Shanghai. The new wheat harvest is very good, and large quantities are arriving in Shanghai from various places, so the market sentiment is very weak. Traders and brokers are strongly hedging, and prices are falling uniformly for all months. The closing prices were down by 0.05 yuan for July, down by 0.06 yuan each for August and September, down by 0.04 yuan for October, and down by 0.06 yuan for November. New wheat also arrived in the Pudong area, with 325 bags priced at 4 yuan, which was purchased by the Shanghai factory. Because there were not many arrivals and the quality was good, it was traded at the railway station.

After the early small harvest this year, few shipments have arrived in Shanghai. Yesterday, 83 bags of new small-grain broad beans from Hankou arrived in the market. The quality was still good, with an opening price of 3.75 yuan. However, the future market is unlikely to be stable due to weak demand. New rapeseed from Jiujiang, which arrived yesterday, also went on sale, with a price of 6.35 yuan. 80 bags of new Wuhu cowpeas were sold to foreign firms at prices above 7 yuan. Qing broad beans from Minhang are in short supply due to limited sources, and the market was firm this morning. 400 bags of Ningbo broad beans continued to arrive, and were sold at 5.40 yuan, continuing to be purchased by the Fuzhou group.

Essays

Fifty Million U.S. Dollars 263

— Geng

This is probably something everyone would like to hear: the Chinese government will have a large income, namely the 50 million U.S. dollars that Finance Minister Song signed for from the U.S. Reconstruction Finance Corporation.

The story is that Song borrowed this huge sum from the U.S. on the condition that American cotton and wheat be purchased on the spot to alleviate our cotton and wheat shortages. It is believed that this loan will benefit both parties, as it can promote the sale of surplus American products and encourage Chinese people to use American cotton and wheat. The repayment period is three years, with a 5% interest rate for extensions.

Our country is currently facing a severe financial crisis, scraping the bottom of the barrel. Has it received the grace of the U.S., a savior? And must it be converted into cotton and wheat on the spot? We, the common people who "have breakfast but no dinner" and "can cover our shame but not our bodies," how can we not be well-fed and sing with full bellies? However, it always feels like it's never easy to get involved with transactions with high-nosed, blue-eyed people. If you insist on getting involved, the result will definitely be like what the Ministry of Education approves: "always losing out." And after losing out, if the other party or a third party asks, you can only force a smile and repeatedly say, "Thank you, thank you, very good, very good!"

Take the flood relief wheat from a few years ago as an example. The initial huge figures of tens of thousands were enough to make some people rejoice, especially those disaster victims who were crying in agony. But what was the result? The loan became wheat, and the wheat became the loan again. From the West to the East, from Beijing and Shanghai to the inland, after these manipulations and magic, how much actual benefit did the disaster victims truly receive? But the status of debtor, regardless of whether you were a victim or not, all compatriots have already earned it effortlessly. Now, it's like dripping molten iron on raw flesh, adding another "50 million U.S. dollars." I fear that from now on, debt will be added to debt, interest will generate interest, and even unborn descendants will have to preemptively accept "working for others for free."

Taking a step back, last year's bumper harvest led to low grain prices harming farmers. The facts are clear. Where did the "wheat shortage" come from? Even the so-called "cotton shortage" has not been widely discussed. I still need to investigate.

Continuous Wind and Rain Overnight 265

Flowers blooming in the courtyard, bathed in water,

Unexpectedly dense rain and slanting wind,

Continuous nights, my soul has no reliable grounding,

In a silk lined garment, I encounter Xishi at Ruoye Creek.

Also

Wind and rain overnight assault these flowers,

Who laments the jade faces fallen to the ground?

Summoning Lin Daiyu from the realm of medicine,

Again, I see affectionate tears like hemp.

The Evolution of "Long-Term" 266

— Bing

An ancient proverb says: "When a sage appears, the Yellow River will run clear." Whether this is absurd or not, let's leave it aside for now. Let's talk about the current state of affairs, where "long-term" has emerged, and China is in great turmoil. Looking at past history and examining reality, there is not a single discrepancy, not a single deviation.

Since our Mr. Sun Yat-sen raised the banner of overthrowing the Qing Dynasty and called for revolution, if we extend our hand and count down our thumb one by one, it has been fully fifty years. During this period, there have been many disturbances, and the country has turned countless somersaults. But even now, everyone says that the revolution has not succeeded, except for the veterans who are already chanting scriptures and worshiping Buddha, cherishing the legacy of the past, and enjoying their peaceful lives.

This, I fear, is the origin of "long-term," or at least the author assumes so: the past has been fifty years, and no one can say how many years it will take for the revolution to truly succeed. Long-term, long-term, the Chinese revolution can be considered the number one long-term project.

Following the "long-term revolution," there has been a set of "long-term recuperation," roughly since the fifteenth and sixteenth years of the Republic. This prelude generally unfolds like this: Among important figures, differences in political views are inevitable. Once there are differences, there will inevitably be open and covert struggles. As a result, one side fails and the other side succeeds. The losers become disheartened, retire from politics, move far away to foreign lands, or retreat to seclusion, and invariably say, "long-term recuperation." In reality, what kind of tricks are played after this prelude can only be recalled by the reader from past objective facts.

"Long-term" ultimately has a source and is inherited. Seeing it, it has already been glorified with the times. The Japanese soldiers, regardless of the impropriety, started from the September 18th Incident the year before last, seized our Shenyang, and have been advancing steadily since then, then the entire province of Fengtian, then Heilongjiang, then the entire Northeast, then all the regions north of the Great Wall, and even Pingjin nearly faced a dangerous situation. Fortunately, our authorities have finally awakened, wagged their tails, and yielded. These days, it seems like the clouds have been parted and we can see the blue sky again, the wind is not too strong and the cranes are not crying, and the storm has not engulfed the entire city. However, our authorities do not yield at heart. "Long-term resistance," is this not the current great policy for resisting humiliation? From September 18th until now, and perhaps until the endless future, in every occasion, is it not the sound of "long-term," "long-term," "long-term resistance" filling our ears?

"Long-term" has already been greatly glorified by being applied to resistance to defend the country, and it seems that there is no more brilliant magic weapon. The reality is not so.

For several days, I have been running around outside. The first time, on North Sichuan Road, I encountered two children carrying a cloth banner advertisement as large as a national flag, parading in the street. The subtitle read:

×× Shoe Company

Long-Term Mega Sale

丨Opportunity Not to Be Missed丨

At that time, I looked at it again and again and felt that the phrase "Opportunity Not to Be Missed" was superfluous and actually contradicted the word "Long-Term." For several days, on Bazilu, outside of the Waituo Bridge, I encountered it twice again, and the phrase "Opportunity Not to Be Missed" was still there. I wanted to go up and offer advice, that even changing it to "Why not come?" would be better. But I deeply fear that those two children are unteachable, afraid of bad luck, and inviting trouble. I dare not, I dare not, so I just let it go.

From this, we can see that "long-term" is not only a great scripture for resisting humiliation and saving the country, but it has actually become a magic weapon for merchants to attract business. How it will evolve in the future is truly something that no one can predict.

Turning back to extensively checking Mr. Wang Yunwu's Great Dictionary and the Revised Edition of the Dictionary, neither has an annotation on the "long-term" great scripture, which is deeply regrettable. I hope lexicographers will have something to add to it in the future.

To bring the conversation back, since "long-term has emerged, China is in great turmoil," readers, please look at China today!

Two Trips to Wusong 267

— Jing Shu

Even I find it strange. I've almost become accustomed to waking up early, but for some reason, today, when I was going to visit Wusong, I woke up especially late—I opened my eyes and it was already five minutes past seven. I jumped out of bed and heard the raindrops outside the window hitting the glass with a crisp sound.

Because I was one of the people responsible, even though we had an agreement that "it would be canceled if it rained," I felt it was still necessary to run to the station. So I quickly washed my face, made a phone call, and called for a car. Fortunately, I arrived at the station at 7:20, twenty minutes before the train was scheduled to leave. In the crowd, I happily found Cheng Yi and Hui Cheng, each carrying a basket of picnic snacks. I asked them, "Has everyone come?" They briefly answered, "Just the two of us."

"Go, go! We'll go even if we have only one companion, let alone now that we have three!" This was our common intention, so we walked into the carriage without hesitation.

As we walked onto the beach of Fort Baoshan, the raindrops became even more intense. Hui Cheng and I had hats, but Cheng Yi's head was bare, so I handed him my raincoat and told him to wear it on his head. So we continued walking, singing marching songs all the way to the end of Fort Baoshan.

The rain was attacking us non-stop, and the wind was also howling and roaring as if it was helping the evil.

Our thin clothes were soaked, our faces were covered with glistening water droplets, and our bodies felt a slight chill; but we didn't feel depressed, we absolutely didn't resent, curse, or hope, we just asked the heavens. We just felt, "Oh, how interesting!"

We wandered around in the wind and rain for a long time, and we took several photos of each other with mirror boxes. Our stomachs were rumbling, so we went to a small teahouse and took out bread and canned food to eat greedily.

At twelve o'clock, we had already walked onto the avenue from Fort Baoshan to Baoshan County. The sky was slowly clearing up, and the number of tourists on the road was gradually increasing. In fact, we didn't feel any pain or itching to whether the sky was clear or raining: the number of tourists did not affect our mood at all, because, you think, you close your eyes and quietly think about it, how beautiful is the seaside on a rainy day, and how poetic is it to stroll along the seaside in the rain! That's enough to satisfy people, how could we say we feel lonely or unhappy?

Because Cheng Yi still had some trivial matters to attend to, he suggested going home early, and we naturally agreed with him because we thought we had gotten reasonably fatigued. When we stepped back into Zhabei, it was already three o'clock.

On the way back and forth, on the train, we passed through the battlefield where the "January 28th" War took place a few years ago. There, broken walls and ruins were everywhere. We stretched our heads out to look, look, and look, we passed one place and then another, and we were all thinking, but we never learned the irrelevant lamentations of the literati, or imitated the unpromising sighs of the weak. We only thought this: The threat of imperialism to us will only increase our "anti-

Page 20

Imperialist" sentiment and strengthen our "anti-Imperialist" determination! Besides, the gains of the imperialists are limited and superficial. Yes, at present, the only way out for our nation is to unite and fight on the organized "anti-Imperialist" battle line. What other way is there?

The Principal's Nose 268

— Yi Li

"The long-nosed one is coming."

Whenever the principal came, we would always spread the word like this, not out of fear, but because we found it amusing.

The principal's nose was indeed very long, about an inch high and half a foot long, standing trembling in the air. Whenever he was furious with his subordinates, this nose would always vibrate strangely in the air, vibrating so much that you would sometimes be terrified, fearing that it would fall off.

When you meet him, the first thing that makes you recognize him is the length of his nose; then you notice his two thick lips twitching tightly, his words slurred and incomprehensible, and everything else.

Friends who came to the school to find us for the first time would always exclaim in surprise: "Your principal's nose is so long!"

Because the number of people who came to find us was large, the number of times we heard such words was also quite a lot, to the point that we were embarrassed and instead blamed the length of this nose for being a stain on the school. However, sometimes we would think, "Maybe our school will soon become famous because of this nose." Because our school, to tell the truth, is nothing special in the city. So we were very comforted, forgetting all the things that looked down on him, and even hoped that he would continue to sit in that chair and calculate the school accounts all day long.

Shop Assistant Communication: Break Time 269

Editor:

I am currently an apprentice in a money shop, and I only studied up to junior high school. My knowledge is shallow, and I am afraid that I will not be able to gain a foothold in society in the future, so I have obtained my parents' consent to attend Russian language classes at ×× night school. However, due to working hard all day long, coupled with mental state reasons, my body has deteriorated; whenever I read, I feel distracted, and after a while, I feel sleepy. After studying for several months, the result is equal to zero. I think that if this continues, it will not be a long-term solution.

I get up at six o'clock every day to practice calligraphy; I go to work at nine o'clock until four o'clock in the afternoon. I go to school to read at seven o'clock, and I can't return to the shop until 9:45. What time can I take a nap to make my energy strong in the evening? Or what kind of energizing medicine is there? The one that is cheap and works quickly is the most suitable. I hope the teacher can guide me! With this, I wish you peace, student Qian Qingshi respectfully.

Editor's Note: An adult needs about eight hours of sleep every day. If he has eight hours of sleep and still feels unenergized, then there must be other reasons, not because he sleeps too little. Now, Mr. Qian gets up at six o'clock every day and, if he goes to bed immediately after 9:45 in the evening, then he still has eight hours of sleep; logically, it is enough. However, when you are in bed between ten o'clock and six o'clock, you should dispel all distracting thoughts: be sure not to let the imagination run wild. So we cannot agree that you want to find a time to sleep briefly during the day. This is not only unnecessary, but also impossible in reality—too early is unnecessary; too late will lead to insomnia at night: and what would it be like for a person with a job to sleep during the day?

We advise you to have appropriate exercise between 6:00 AM and 9:00 AM, or between 4:00 PM and 7:00 PM. When we are doing things in the writing room, the brain is working, and the limbs are almost completely resting. When we exercise, the opposite is true. The limbs are fully exercised, and the brain rests completely. This way, during the day, the brain and limbs take turns resting; then, with eight hours of sleep at night, your energy will definitely be strong. As for energizing drugs, we dare not introduce them. A person without illness does not need to take medicine; and most energizing drugs contain stimulants, which are harmful if used for a long time. If you do not have symptoms of illness, we advise you not to try them; even if you feel that you already have symptoms of illness and have to resort to medicine, you must ask a doctor for diagnosis. For "patent medicines" in pharmacies, it is best not to take them.

Fiction

The Life of the Fifth Consort (Continuation 27) 271

— Ling He

Twenty-five, 250 yuan

Everyone needs a way to pass the time. Since the young master was no longer as clingy as before, the Fifth Consort's only pastime was reading "Dream of the Red Chamber." Like every young lady, the Fifth Consort hoped to win the favor of the handsome Baoyu, but she did not agree with Daiyu's hopeless weeping. However, she admired Wang Xifeng's character very much. But she was ashamed; could she really be as shrewd and capable as Sister Feng? In the end, she had no full confidence. Thinking of this, she gently put down the book and stared blankly out the window. Then, she picked up Zhang Wenbin's photo from beside her pillow and sighed heavily.

An old maid came in with a piece of paper, saying that there was a car waiting outside. The Fifth Consort took the paper and saw that it was a car sent by the Second Consort to pick her up for mahjong. She thought, "This is a great opportunity to get to know the Second Consort." So she immediately dressed up, left at once, got into the car, and drove off.

As the driver drove up to the Second Consort's house, he honked the horn several times. An inspector immediately opened the iron gate to welcome them, driving all the way to the front of the stone steps to stop. The Fifth Consort got out of the car in her cloak, and a maid immediately came forward to serve her. Walking into the Second Consort's bedroom, she saw women she had never seen before. But she was very smart, knowing that the one whose Mandarin was not very pure was the Second Consort, even though she was completely dressed as a Chinese wife. Then, through the Second Consort's introduction, she learned that the two young ladies were the eldest and second Misses who had just come from Beijing. Naturally, these two young ladies were very decent, especially the eldest Miss, whose short hair covering her forehead was even more charming, but the second Miss, holding a pair of all-white kittens in her hands, was also very docile and cute.

Everyone exchanged pleasantries while cracking melon seeds and puffing on cigarettes. Soon, they moved to the outer room and sat down at the mahjong table. The surface of the sandalwood table was covered with a silk tablecloth, nothing special, but the mahjong set with green jade inlaid on the outside was something the Fifth Consort's family did not have. Thinking carefully about it, she couldn't help but feel ashamed.

After a game of mahjong, probably because she was out of luck, the Fifth Consort lost more than two hundred and fifty yuan. However, the Fifth Consort knew that if she hadn't intentionally let the Second Consort, who was her next player, eat a few more tiles, the Second Consort would have had no way to win money. Moreover, after a game of mahjong, the Second Consort actually became very close to her. How could this be bought with a hundred or two hundred yuan? What did a mere two hundred and fifty yuan amount to? Therefore, even though our Fifth Consort lost money, she still smiled and talked generously.

At the dinner table, Minister Su was very happy because they could be so harmonious, and furthermore,

After dinner, the Second Consort insisted that he personally send the Fifth Consort back, so he felt even more that his good fortune was not small.

The Twenty-Second Year of the Republic of China

Film Special

The Making of the Horror Film "King Kong" 272

— Luo Fen

Unmasking the Western Mirror - So It Is!

In the film industry of 1933, many horror films have appeared. The most terrifying of these is "King Kong" from RKO Pictures. Hollywood's film industry believes that "King Kong" is the most terrifying work in horror films, enough to overwhelm all "Dragon Tiger Fight," "The Lost World," "The Old Dark House," "Frankenstein," etc. But how was this film made? For example, a very large ape, as tall as the sky, killed many people, and even took a woman away (played by the actress Fay Wray). Later, many methods were used to kill this giant ape and save the woman's life. When the giant ape climbed to the top of the highest building in New York, many planes were used to bomb it, and even one plane was destroyed by the giant ape. How was such a giant ape filmed?

The filming of "King Kong" is completely fake. It relies on the skills of the cinematographer and set designer, using complex composite photography to piece together several scenes. It also relies on the use of light, without revealing any flaws. The audience will never feel that this film is fake. The technical ingenuity is enough to be called a masterpiece of filming techniques in 1933.

In the key scene of "King Kong," the giant ape climbs to the top of a tall building in New York, holding the woman in its palm. Planes bomb it in the sky. This scene was filmed using seven pieces of film spliced together. First, the scenery of the New York sky was filmed on a high building in New York, with all the high rooftops in the film. Second, the situation of the planes flying in the sky was filmed. Then, the first and second films were spliced together and re-filmed into one film. Third, the huge ape was filmed. A very small model ape was used, and then it was spliced together with the first composite film. Finally, a side view of a woman lying down was filmed, and then matched with the second composite film. In this way, one layer upon another, a total of seven films were used, and four composite re-filming procedures were spent. As long as the effort is deep enough, an iron ruler can be ground into a needle. The effort is naturally not small, but the results cannot be said to be not great.

In addition to the giant ape, there are also four kinds of monsters, unusually ferocious, the most terrifying animals in the ancient world, which were also filmed using models, spliced and re-filmed with other real-life films. Although "King Kong" has no meaning at all, its filming work is enough to open a new era in the art world.

Audience Opinions

Review of "Innocence" 273

— Bacon

Because it focuses on elaborating on innocence, a modern dancer does not love the warlord/division commander who is rich and round-faced but accepts the diligence of a small mustache and still remembers her old love for the painter. Such an innocent dancer cannot be found in today's society. And the secondary important character in this theme, the painter, is also extremely stubborn and simple. This film tries its best to think from the opposite side, but it can't find anything commendable, while the various dark secrets of society, such as prostitution, assassination, and the temptation of money and flesh, are performed vividly.

The expressions of the actors are just so-so for the protagonist, and the rest are even more mediocre.

The identity of the dance hall manager doesn't seem to require showing off humor. Turning a somersault when kicking guests out is even more abrupt. Such an interlude is counterproductive. The facial makeup of several gamblers has many flaws. The dance hall manager seems to be tailing, and then he goes to the Wei family to mediate, which leads to the dancer's origins very unnaturally. The division commander bribes the foster father and secretly enters the dancer's bedroom, and is assassinated. It only takes one knife, which seems insufficient. The dancer is stabbed, and at least there should be a cry for help. Wouldn't people only a door away hear it? Furthermore, she is stabbed and falls outside the door, which seems to be the door of the dance hall, but in the end, she is picked up by a drunk, which doesn't seem like the door of the dance hall. This location is somewhat vague. What is the point of the painter carrying a portrait and running around? It is also inexplicable.

Talking About "Innocence" 274

— Yu Jiaqing

"Innocence" is such a "noble" and "honorable" word. This is a production of the fourth factory of Lianhua. The general idea of this film is about a poor painter who falls in love with a lonely woman. She is taken care of by a gambling addict, who is outwardly her father, but in reality, she is his "slave" and his "source of income" because he is forced to take his daughter to be a dancer due to cheating in the gambling hall. Because she is too popular, a jealous incident occurs. When the poor painter finds out about this incident, he breaks up with her, ridicules her, and says she is not "innocent" or "pure," but until her death, she remains "innocent" and "pure."

The plot is very ordinary, without any instruction, and the director has no special skills. There are many minor flaws. The photography lighting is blurry in several places, and the scenery is also very simple.

The actors, such as Yin Mingzhu, perform well, but playing a seventeen or eighteen-year-old young girl seems too inappropriate for her status. Luo Keming's expressions are good in the first half, but lacking in facial expressions in the second half. Wei Guang is too much, and Han Langen's humor is somewhat contrived. The rest have no special features, and the actors are all mediocre.

Impressions After Watching "Innocence" 275

— Shi Bin

The theme of this film is somewhat elusive. Although it is named "Innocence," after watching it, one cannot help but feel that it is not "clear" and not "white."

The subtitles tell the audience: "Pipa is a good woman, she is willing to work, but not willing to be a dancing girl embraced by the public." But I see her performance on the screen seems to be greatly contrary to her ambition, isn't that a noteworthy loophole?

The painter Xiao originally loved Pipa very much, but later he learned that she was imprisoned! When he saw Pipa, he not only did not comfort her, but actually blamed her indiscriminately. Is this also for the sake of loving her?

As for the expressions of the actors, Ms. Yin Mingzhu performs best, but there is one thing, Ms. Yin's youth has passed with time. In this film, it seems that she is not suitable for the role of the young girl, Pipa, but it is to her credit that she can fully describe the naivety and vitality of the young girl. The rest, such as Min De Zhang, are very successful, Luo Kepeng is just so-so, and Han Langen is somewhat overly humorous!

In short, the plot of this film has failed, the expressions of the actors are commendable, and the director's skills are also worthy of admiration.

After Watching "Innocence" 276

— Ya Hua

"Innocence" is directed by Dan Duyu, and he is indeed very capable of using his talent to unfold each scene very actively, making the audience feel satisfied. However, the pacing is too fast and superficial, and the lighting is also somewhat stagnant.

Due to the unsound structure of the script of "Innocence" and those unnecessary forced insertions, the audience cannot feel tension and cannot get a deep impression.

The screenwriter of "Innocence" wanted to write the (Pipa) in the play as a poor girl, so at the beginning of the film, it is written that eighteen years ago, Pipa was still in swaddling clothes, and her father was imprisoned, so he entrusted Pipa to Wei Guang as a foster daughter. Wei Guang is a gambling and brutal man, so Pipa's situation is naturally very miserable.

Yin Mingzhu, who plays Pipa, has not seen vitality in the action of playing a young girl, but the later dance girl is very good. Pipa's lover, the painter Xiao (played by Luo Keming), performs very ordinarily. Because his performance is ordinary, and the script is scattered, the drama's "focus of love" could not be fully performed. Since the center of gravity of the whole play is lost, each scene after that cannot be natural.

The section where Pipa is lured to the Western Hotel by Ma Shichang is filmed very well, but Pipa's dancing appearance kills Ma Shichang out of jealousy, because it does not clearly write out how passionately Wuyong is in love with Pipa, so it feels abrupt, and the audience does not know why the dancing appearance wants to kill Ma Shichang.

The plot originally wanted to write that Pipa was still chaste until her death, but the screen did not clearly write it out, so the audience only felt that her death was unfortunate and did not have some pity.

In short, Dan Jun's use of photography skills, scenery, and many small movements are worthy of appreciation, but it is a pity that it failed in the script.

Tianyi's Two "Trilogies" 277

— Cao Yang

Tianyi Film Company has recently been actively transforming. In the future, its productions will completely abandon the love themes of "Pursuit" and "The Lost Orchid Valley," and resolutely embark on the path needed by movie audiences, striving for "anti-feudal" and "anti-imperial" performances. It particularly focuses on the future of Chinese women and the exposure of the lives of the working masses.

Tianyi is currently working hard on two "trilogies"丨丨 (1) "Dusk," "Dawn," "Vitality" (2) "Dead End," "Bloody Road," "Living Road." This news should make us somewhat happy, because it clearly shows that the transformation of Tianyi Company is an entire great transformation, and it is courageously advancing towards the path of true film art.

It is heard that "Dusk" and "Dawn" are being filmed, and "Vitality" has been released in the capital and will return to Shanghai soon. In this film, director Shao Zuiweng, protagonist Chen Yumei, and supporting actors Yuan Meiyun, Lu Lixia, Xiao Zhengzhong, Zhang Zhenduo, etc., are all performing a new technique. Some people say, "The leading actress Chen Yumei has never worked so hard before. Here, she has used all her current strength." This film is definitely worth our attention. The theme of "Vitality" is: A woman is married to a bourgeois husband, and usually suffers all kinds of anger and humiliation from that man, so she realizes the path she should take. She finally unites with the women of the working class, jumps out of the golden dream's bed, and advances to the road of "vitality." Detailed content has been published in the issue of this publication on April 25.

Claudette Colbert's Fist 278

The leading actress in "Cleopatra," Ms. Claudette Colbert, is only five feet five inches tall and weighs one hundred and three pounds. It can be said that she is a petite and exquisite girl. Who would believe that she is proficient in boxing? But one day, she played a shrew in (I Cover the Waterfront) and had to fight the other party. The director ordered Claudette to treat the other party very rudely. Claudette said, "I don't want to really hit her. I'm afraid it will be too realistic."

The director looked at her and said, "Don't worry. Even if you hit harder, you won't hurt her." Claudette smiled and prepared to fight.

"Camera! Action!" shouted a voice. Claudette saw the other party running over, and calmly aimed at her face and punched her hard. The other party fell to the ground and was injured. It took more than ten minutes to wake her up.

"Good friend, do you really hate me so much?"

Film Novel Girls in Uniform Part 3 279

— Xin Fu

Produced by German Film Company, starring a joint cast of female actors

"One, two, three, turn left! One, two, three, turn left and walk! What is this? It turns out that the students are lining up, waiting for the principal's speech! In the center of the auditorium, there is a lecture platform. Hundreds of students are arranged in a semicircular formation in front of the lecture platform. Several slave-like teachers also stood on both sides. After a while, the self-proclaimed female principal, wearing glasses with lenses, and holding a cane, walked step by step onto the lecture platform. As usual, she ordered the students to sing a sunflower poem song first, and then began her speech. But talking about it, it's just the old clichés of "obeying discipline" and "obeying orders." Recently, she probably found some private letters in the school! So in the end, she said with force! "Whether it is sending out or receiving letters, they must follow the law, otherwise they will be severely punished." Manny Nella saw the principal's attitude in the crowd, and couldn't help but feel chills again.

"This child is so pitiful, she doesn't have a mother. I see that she's been frowning all day long since she came here." A maid of Pei's was cleaning her room, while muttering to herself. "Who are you talking about," Pei asked, "isn't it that Miss Mannella!" the maid replied. Pei Bai heard this and paused for a while. Then she said to the maid! "Go find her, I have something to say to her." The maid agreed and went away with a limp.

After a while, Manny Nella really followed the maid in. Pei Bai was originally sitting there looking at the coupons. When she saw Manny Nella, she stood up with a smile and walked to Manny's side. She shook Manny's hand and said, "Mannella, are you not used to anything when you first came here? But it will be better after staying for a while. You have to be happy, don't be pessimistic! Promise me"? To Manny Nella, who has not enjoyed the love of her mother for many years; to a girl who is pursuing love, in such an unfamiliar place with no relatives, how could these words not hit her heart! So she was grateful, she shed tears, and finally she lay on Pei Bai's arm and cried bitterly!

Dang! Dang! Dang! The bedtime bell rang! The students put on their nightgowns one by one and walked to the bedside. Ms. Pei Bai walked into the room under her jurisdiction, turned off the lights first. Then she said to everyone, "Be quiet, I'll give you that good-night kiss!" The many students squatted on the edge of the bed, holding the bed railing with both hands, as if young birds were waiting for old birds to feed them, raising their heads, waiting for Pei Bai to give them a kiss. The last one was Manny Nella! Her heart suddenly became excited; her enthusiasm was boiling in her chest; her tired autumn waves shot straight at Pei Bai. She couldn't help but hug Pei Bai, and put her mouth against Pei Bai's mouth, kissing it hard, before falling asleep quietly. (To be continued)
